1. list all the flights that arrive at DAL from various cities
P: what flights from any city land at DAL
P: show me the flights into DAL
P: show me the flights arriving at DAL
P: list all the flights that arrive at DAL
P: list all the arriving flights at DAL
P: what flights land at DAL
P: show me the flights to DAL
P: list all the landings at DAL
P: list all flights arriving at DAL
P: list all the flights that fly into DAL
P: list all the flights that arrive at DAL airport
P: show me all flights arriving at DAL from other airports
P: show me the flights from all airports to DAL
P: show me the flights arriving at DAL from all other airports
P: show me flights from all airports to DAL
P: show me the flights arriving at DAL from other airports
P: show me the flights to DAL from all other airports

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t3 ON t4.to_airport = t3.airport_code WHERE t3.airport_code = "DAL";

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "TACOMA" AND t4.day_number = 10 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "BURBANK";

3. what is the most expensive one way fare from BOSTON to ATLANTA on AA

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t4 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t5.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t4.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t2.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id AND t3.airline_code = "AA" AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t6.day_name = "SATURDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE t4.city_name = "NEW YORK" AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI";

6. i'd like to see flights from BALTIMORE to ATLANTA that arrive before 1200 and i'd like to see flights from DENVER to ATLANTA that arrive before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) OR ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) ) AND t5.arrival_time < 1200;

7. do you have an 1300 flight from BOSTON to ATLANTA
P: i would like a flight from BOSTON to ATLANTA departing at 1300
P: do you have a flight leaving BOSTON at 1300 going to ATLANTA
P: i need a flight from BOSTON to ATLANTA leaving at 1300

P: i would like a flight between BOSTON and ATLANTA on any day at one in the afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t5.departure_time = 1300 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

8. can you list all round trip flights from ATLANTA to DENVER and then to DALLAS
P: is there a round trip flight from ATLANTA to DALLAS via DENVER

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t10 ON t10.stop_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t10.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t5.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t2.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t6.city_name = "ATLANTA";

9. does AA fly from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO

P: does AA fly between ATLANTA and SAN FRANCISCO
P: does AA fly to SAN FRANCISCO from ATLANTA

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t1.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA";

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.from_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "CHICAGO" AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t5.airline_code = "AA";

11. are there any nonstop flights leaving from DENVER arriving in BALTIMORE on 7 7

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) AND t5.day_number = 6 AND t5.month_number = 7 AND t5.year = 1991 ) OR t4.year = 1991 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.day_number = 7 ) AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

12. are there any flights between PITTSBURGH and BALTIMORE using a J31 aircraft

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( t5.aircraft_code = "J31" AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

13. what does LS stand for for meals
P: what does LS designate as a meal
P: what does the meal code LS stand for
P: what is the meaning of meal code LS
P: explain meal codes LS
P: what does LS stand for

SELECT DISTINCT compartment , meal_code , meal_description , meal_number FROM food_service WHERE meal_code = "LS";

14. what are the flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE returning on tuesday 5 10
P: please list the flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE arriving 5 day_number1
P: list the flights arriving in BALTIMORE from DENVER on 5 day_number1
P: show me the flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE which arrive at BALTIMORE on monday
P: show me all the flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE arriving 5 10

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t2.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t8.day_name = t5.day_name WHERE ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t5.day_number = 10 AND t5.month_number = 5 AND t5.year = 1991 ) AND t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t1.state_name = "state_name0";

15. i need the cost of a ticket going from SAN FRANCISCO to DENVER a BUSINESS class ticket on UA
P: what is the BUSINESS fare between SAN FRANCISCO and DENVER on UA
P: what is the price of BUSINESS class from SAN FRANCISCO to DENVER on UA
P: show BUSINESS class fares on UA from SAN FRANCISCO to DENVER
P: show BUSINESS class fares from SAN FRANCISCO to DENVER on UA

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( t6.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t2.class_type = "BUSINESS" AND t4.airline_code = "UA";

16. is there a flight between SAN FRANCISCO and BOSTON with a stopover at DALLAS FORT WORTH
P: i need a flight from SAN FRANCISCO to BOSTON via DALLAS FORT WORTH
P: i'm looking for a flight from SAN FRANCISCO to BOSTON with a stopover in DALLAS FORT WORTH
P: is there a flight from SAN FRANCISCO to BOSTON making a stopover in DALLAS FORT WORTH
P: yes i'm looking for a flight between SAN FRANCISCO and BOSTON with a stopover in DALLAS FORT WORTH do you have one of those
P: is there a flight between SAN FRANCISCO and BOSTON with a stopover in DALLAS FORT WORTH

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t10 ON t10.stop_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_stop AS t11 ON t1.flight_id = t10.flight_id JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t11.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t11.stop_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t9.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO";

17. list the takeoffs and landings at DAL
P: please list all the takeoffs and landings for DAL
P: list all flights arriving and departing at DAL
P: list the flights that arrive and depart from DAL airport
P: list all the takeoffs and landings at DAL
P: what flights takeoff and land at DAL
P: please list all the arriving and departing flights from DAL
P: list all the takeoffs and landings at DAL airport
P: list all takeoffs and landings at DAL
P: list all flights at DAL
P: please list the flights taking off and landing on DAL airport
P: show me the flights to and from DAL

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight AS t3 JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t2 ON t3.from_airport = t2.airport_code WHERE ( t1.airport_code = "DAL" ) OR ( t2.airport_code = "DAL" );

18. is there TAXI service at ONT airport
P: is there a TAXI service available from the ONT airport
P: what TAXI are available next sunday from ONT airport
P: is there TAXI service at the ONT airport

SELECT DISTINCT t2.transport_type FROM ground_service AS t2 JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.airport_code = t1.airport_code WHERE t1.airport_code = "ONT" AND t2.transport_type = "TAXI";

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE t6.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t2.class_type = "COACH";

21. in BOSTON BALTIMORE i would like information on ground transportation
P: what kinds of ground transportation is available in BOSTON BALTIMORE
P: ground transportation in BOSTON and BALTIMORE
P: show me ground transportation in BOSTON and in BALTIMORE

SELECT DISTINCT t3.transport_type FROM ground_service AS t3 JOIN city AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t3.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) OR ( t1.city_name = "BALTIMORE" );

22. i'd like flights on AA from PHILADELPHIA philadelphia to DALLAS arriving before 1145
P: i'd like flights on AA from PHILADELPHIA to DALLAS arriving before 1145

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t5.arrival_time < 1145 ) AND t5.airline_code = "AA";

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE t3.city_name = "SEATTLE" AND t2.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY";

24. what airlines from WASHINGTON DC to COLUMBUS

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t3.state_code = "DC" AND t2.city_name = "COLUMBUS";

25. which airlines fly from BOSTON to WASHINGTON DC

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t2.state_code = "DC";

26. i would like a flight from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO leaving at 1200 on 11 7
P: i would like to fly from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO on the morning of 11 7 leaving at 1200
P: is there a flight leaving at 1200 from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO on 11 7 1991
P: i would like flights between ATLANTA and SAN FRANCISCO on 11 7 departing at one in the afternoon
P: 1200 flight on 11 7 from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO
P: i would like a flight leaving from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO at 1200 on 11 7
P: what flights are available from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO on 11 7 1200
P: i'd like to go from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO at 1200 o'clock saturday night
P: i would like a flight from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO on 11 7 at 1200
P: is there a flight from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO on 11 7 at 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 7 AND t4.month_number = 11 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time = 1200 ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA";

27. are there any nonstop flights from BURBANK to DENVER that arrive before 1800
P: list nonstop flights from BURBANK to DENVER which arrive before 1800
P: list nonstop flights from BURBANK to DENVER arriving by 1800

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "DENVER" AND t5.arrival_time <= 1800 ) AND t4.city_name = "BURBANK" ) AND t5.stops = 0;

28. i'd like to fly nonstop from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE and get there at 1900
P: i need a flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE nonstop arriving at 1900 please

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t5.arrival_time = 1900 ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.stops = 0;

29. give me WEDNESDAY nonstop flights from OAKLAND to BOSTON
P: are there any nonstop flights from OAKLAND to BOSTON on WEDNESDAY
P: i want a direct flight from OAKLAND to BOSTON that leaves on a WEDNESDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t6.day_name = "WEDNESDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

30. what is the type of aircraft for CO flight 1209
P: what aircraft is CO 1209

SELECT DISTINCT t2.aircraft_code FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t2 ON t1.aircraft_code = t2.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence WHERE t3.airline_code = "CO" AND t3.flight_number = 1209;

31. can you give me information on transportation from the airport in DENVER to downtown DENVER
P: what ground transportation is available at the DENVER airport
P: please give grounds transportation at DENVER airport
P: what ground transportation is available at DENVER airport
P: fine can you give me information on ground transportation in DENVER to downtown
P: show me the ground transportation in the DENVER airport
P: tell me about ground transportation in DENVER airport
P: show me a list of ground transportation at DENVER airport
P: i need your help with information on ground transportation from the airport in DENVER to downtown
P: show me the ground transportation to DENVER
P: i need information on ground transportation from the airport in DENVER
P: what type of ground transportation is available at DENVER airport
P: what kind of ground transportation is available in DENVER
P: can you help me with ground transportation information i need to get from the airport in DENVER to downtown DENVER
P: how do i get downtown from the DENVER airport
P: please give ground transportation at DENVER airport

SELECT DISTINCT t4.transport_type FROM airport AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN ground_service AS t4 ON t4.airport_code = t3.airport_code WHERE t2.city_name = "DENVER";

32. on US how many flights leaving OAKLAND on 7 27 to BOSTON nonstop

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t1.flight_id ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t4.day_number = 27 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t1.airline_code = "US" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t1.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" );

34. find travel arrangements for a round trip flight from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: please show me all round trip flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: give me all the flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO round trip
P: list all round trip flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: what are the round trip flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: i would like to make a round trip between KANSAS CITY and CHICAGO
P: okay could you get me a round trip ticket from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: okay i've got somebody else who wants to take a round trip ticket from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: show me the round trip flights between KANSAS CITY and CHICAGO
P: round trip flights between KANSAS CITY and CHICAGO

P: please show me the round trip flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: list the round trip flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: please show me round trip tickets from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO
P: show me the round trip tickets from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO

P: show me round trips between KANSAS CITY and CHICAGO

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id WHERE ( t4.city_name = "CHICAGO" AND t2.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t5.city_name = "KANSAS CITY";

35. what flights do you have from INDIANAPOLIS to SEATTLE WASHINGTON
P: show me the flights from INDIANAPOLIS to SEATTLE WASHINGTON
P: flight from INDIANAPOLIS to SEATTLE WASHINGTON
P: i'd like a flight from INDIANAPOLIS to SEATTLE WASHINGTON
P: show me the flights that go from INDIANAPOLIS to SEATTLE WASHINGTON
P: flights from INDIANAPOLIS to SEATTLE WASHINGTON

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t3.state_code WHERE t4.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" AND t3.city_name = "SEATTLE" AND t1.state_name = "WASHINGTON";

36. list all flights from WASHINGTON to TAMPA FLORIDA

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t3.state_code WHERE t4.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t4.state_code = "DC" AND t3.city_name = "TAMPA" AND t1.state_name = "FLORIDA";

38. is fare code B the same as BUSINESS class

SELECT DISTINCT fare_basis_code FROM fare_basis WHERE booking_class = "BUSINESS" AND fare_basis_code = "B";

39. all flights and fares from ATLANTA to DALLAS round trip after 12pm less than 1100 dollars
P: all flights from ATLANTA to DALLAS round trip after 12pm less than 1100

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM flight_fare AS t2 JOIN fare AS t7 ON t2.fare_id = t7.fare_id JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t5.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t5.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t5.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare AS t3 ON t1.fare_id = t3.fare_id WHERE ( ( t7.round_trip_cost < 1100 AND t5.departure_time > 1200 ) AND t6.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.round_trip_cost < 1100;

40. i need to spend much of a day on the ground in ATLANTA find me an early flight from BOSTON and the lastest possible flight back from ATLANTA

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t5.departure_time < 1000 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) OR ( ( t3.city_code = t2.city_code AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t1.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code ) AND t4.city_code = t1.city_code AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code );

41. show me all UA FIRST class flights

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM fare AS t2 JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t2.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id WHERE t3.class_type = "FIRST" AND t4.airline_code = "UA";

43. i need a flight tonight from CHARLOTTE to LAS VEGAS with a stop in ST. LOUIS and i want DINNER

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t11 JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t11.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN food_service AS t10 ON t1.flight_days = t11.days_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t11.days_code JOIN flight_stop AS t9 ON t1.flight_id = t9.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t9.stop_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 2359 AND t1.departure_time >= 1800 ) AND t5.day_number = 6 AND t5.month_number = 5 AND t5.year = 1991 ) OR ( ( t1.departure_time <= 600 AND t1.departure_time >= 0 ) AND t5.day_number = 7 AND t5.month_number = 5 AND t5.year = 1991 ) ) AND t10.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t2.city_name = "ST. LOUIS" ) AND t3.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" ) AND t4.city_name = "CHARLOTTE";

44. show me the one way flight from DETROIT to WESTCHESTER COUNTY with the highest fare
P: show me the flight from DETROIT to WESTCHESTER COUNTY with the highest one way fare

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t5.city_name = "DETROIT" AND t4.city_name = "WESTCHESTER COUNTY" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE t4.city_name = "DETROIT" AND t3.city_name = "WESTCHESTER COUNTY" AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t2.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

45. which NW and UA flights go through DENVER before 1200
P: which flights on NW and UA stop in DENVER before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t3 ON t3.stop_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t3.flight_id WHERE ( ( t4.airline_code = "NW" ) OR ( t4.airline_code = "UA" ) ) AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.arrival_time < 1200;

46. what are the most expensive FIRST class tickets between BOSTON and SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t6.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t5.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t6.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE t5.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" );

47. show all WEDNESDAY morning flights from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO
P: what flights are there from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO early on WEDNESDAY mornings

P: show the flights from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO on a WEDNESDAY morning
P: what afternoon flights are available from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO on WEDNESDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t6.day_name = "WEDNESDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

48. i would like to know what type of aircraft will be used on the morning of 7 7 from ATLANTA to BOSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t6.day_number = 7 AND t6.month_number = 7 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200;

49. show flights from DALLAS to SAN FRANCISCO that arrive before 1600

P: give me the flights from DALLAS to SAN FRANCISCO arriving before 1600

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t5.arrival_time <= 1600 ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS";

50. how many passengers can a BOEING 767 hold

51. list all flights from WASHINGTON to ATLANTA late saturday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 2359 AND t1.departure_time >= 1800 ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( ( t1.departure_time <= 1200 AND t1.departure_time >= 0 ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA";

55. i would like to find a flight that goes from LGA airport to SAN JOSE i would like the flight to be on UA and arrive in SAN JOSE around 10pm
P: what flights on UA leave LGA for SAN JOSE and arrive around 10pm

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t3 ON t4.from_airport = t3.airport_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.arrival_time <= 2230 AND t4.arrival_time >= 2130 ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN JOSE" ) AND t3.airport_code = "LGA" ) AND t4.airline_code = "UA";

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "BURBANK" AND t4.day_number = 14 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "CINCINNATI" ) AND t1.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

64. what is the first flight after 800 from BOSTON for SAN FRANCISCO
P: what 's the first flight after 800 leaving BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO
P: what is the first flight after 800 from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t5.departure_time > 800 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code WHERE ( t1.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t5.departure_time > 800 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" );

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t3.departure_time < 1000 ) AND t2.city_name = "MEMPHIS" ) AND t5.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS";

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t5.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t3.airline_code = "US";

72. show me the latest DINNER flight from BALTIMORE to OAKLAND

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t6.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t6.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" );

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time <= 2400 ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER";

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE t5.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t4.round_trip_required = "NO";

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND ( t1.arrival_time <= 1200 AND t1.arrival_time >= 0 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "ST. LOUIS" ) AND t3.city_name = "ST. PAUL";

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.departure_time < 1200 ) AND t4.city_name = "CLEVELAND";

81. what round trip flights between ATLANTA and DENVER qualify for fare code QX

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id WHERE ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t2.fare_basis_code = "QX" AND t2.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t5.city_name = "ATLANTA";

82. what is the earliest flight from ATLANTA to DENVER that serves a meal

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" );

83. of the flights available from DALLAS to BALTIMORE on 12 24 which airline has the least expensive flight
P: which airline offers the cheapest rate going from DALLAS to BALTIMORE on 12 24
P: which airline is the cheapest to fly from DALLAS to BALTIMORE on 12 24

SELECT DISTINCT t9.airline_code FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN days AS t10 ON t3.flight_days = t10.days_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t10.day_name = t6.day_name , airline AS t9 , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t6.day_number = 24 AND t6.month_number = 12 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name WHERE ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t6.day_number = 24 AND t6.month_number = 12 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.airline_code = t9.airline_code AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

88. do you have a night flight from WASHINGTON to BOSTON on 8 27

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t4.day_number = 28 AND t4.month_number = 8 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 27 AND t4.month_number = 8 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t1.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759;

89. flights from BALTIMORE to SAN FRANCISCO on saturday morning on UA

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t4.day_number = 27 AND t4.month_number = 8 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t1.airline_code = "UA";

90. what is the earliest arriving flight from BOSTON to WASHINGTON DC
P: what is the earliest arriving flight between BOSTON and WASHINGTON DC
P: what 's the earliest arriving flight between BOSTON and WASHINGTON DC

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE ( ( from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "BOSTON" ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE ( city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND state_code = "DC" ) ) ) ) AND arrival_time = ( SELECT MIN ( arrival_time ) FROM flight WHERE ( from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "BOSTON" ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE ( city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND state_code = "DC" ) ) ) ) ) );

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "PHOENIX" ) AND t1.airline_code = "AA";

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE t5.city_name = "SAN JOSE" AND t2.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY";

93. show me round trip fares between BOSTON and WASHINGTON
P: list all round trip fares from BOSTON to WASHINGTON

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE t5.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t2.state_code = "DC" AND t4.round_trip_cost is NOT null;

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE ( ( ( t3.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t3.flight_number = 928 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS FORT WORTH";

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t5.city_name = "DENVER" AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

97. i would like a list of the round trip flights between INDIANAPOLIS and ORLANDO on the 27 or the 28 of 12
P: list all round trip flights from INDIANAPOLIS to ORLANDO departing either on 12 27 or on 12 28

SELECT DISTINCT t6.flight_id FROM days AS t14 JOIN date_day AS t10 ON t14.day_name = t10.day_name JOIN flight AS t6 ON t6.flight_days = t14.days_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t6.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t7 ON t2.fare_id = t7.fare_id JOIN flight_fare AS t3 ON t6.flight_id = t3.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t12 ON t6.to_airport = t12.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t11 ON t6.from_airport = t11.airport_code JOIN fare_basis AS t4 ON t7.fare_basis_code = t4.fare_basis_code JOIN days AS t13 ON t4.basis_days = t13.days_code JOIN fare AS t8 ON t3.fare_id = t8.fare_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t12.city_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t11.city_code JOIN date_day AS t9 ON t13.day_name = t9.day_name WHERE ( ( ( ( t10.day_number = 27 AND t10.month_number = 12 AND t10.year = 1991 AND t9.day_number = 27 AND t9.month_number = 12 AND t9.year = 1991 AND t7.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) OR ( t10.day_number = 28 AND t10.month_number = 12 AND t10.year = 1991 AND t9.day_number = 28 AND t9.month_number = 12 AND t9.year = 1991 AND t7.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) ) AND t8.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t5.city_name = "ORLANDO" ) AND t1.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS";

98. list all the flights from CHARLOTTE to ATLANTA that return around 7pm

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t4.state_code WHERE ( ( t2.arrival_time <= 1930 AND t2.arrival_time >= 1830 ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t4.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" AND t1.state_name = "NORTH CAROLINA";

99. what is the latest afternoon flight departing DENVER and arriving in BOSTON on 1 20
P: can you tell me the latest evening flight from DENVER to BOSTON on 1 20
P: show me the last flight available in the evening from DENVER to BOSTON on 1 20

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 );

100. list DAILY flights from OAKLAND to BOSTON using TW
P: list all DAILY flights between OAKLAND and BOSTON using TW

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.airline_code = "TW" ) AND t5.flight_days = "DAILY";

103. show me the cheapest one way flight from DALLAS to SAN FRANCISCO leaving DALLAS after 1600
P: show me the cheapest one way flights from DALLAS to SAN FRANCISCO leaving DALLAS after 1600

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t3.departure_time > 1600 ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.departure_time > 1600 ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

104. show me the type of aircraft that CANADIAN AIRLINES uses
P: show me the aircraft that CANADIAN AIRLINES uses

SELECT DISTINCT t2.basic_type FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t2 ON t1.aircraft_code = t2.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN airline AS t4 ON t3.airline_code = t4.airline_code WHERE t4.airline_name LIKE "CANADIAN AIRLINES";

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "TAMPA" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "TAMPA" );

P: i want a one way ticket from MILWAUKEE to ORLANDO

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id WHERE ( t4.city_name = "ORLANDO" AND t2.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t5.city_name = "MILWAUKEE";

109. is there an airline that advertises having more flights than any other airline

SELECT DISTINCT COUNT ( * ) , airline_code FROM flight GROUP BY airline_code;

110. show me all flights which leave PITTSBURGH tomorrow and arrive in BALTIMORE after 1700 o'clock pm

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.arrival_time > 1700 ) AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

113. what type of aircraft is used on the first flight from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO in the morning
P: what kind of plane is used on the earliest flight from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) AND t2.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t1.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 );

114. give me flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE on UA that offer FIRST class
P: please list all FIRST class flights on UA from DENVER to BALTIMORE
P: please give me the UA flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE that are the FIRST class flights please
P: FIRST class flights on UA from DENVER to BALTIMORE
P: an UA flight FIRST class from DENVER to BALTIMORE
P: show flights FIRST class on UA between DENVER and BALTIMORE
P: does UA provide any FIRST class flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t3 ON t1.fare_id = t3.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t3.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( t6.city_name = "DENVER" AND t5.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t4.airline_code = "UA";

115. what is the round trip fare on US 3724 from BALTIMORE to PHILADELPHIA and return
P: US 3724 BALTIMORE to PHILADELPHIA what is the round trip fare

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t3.flight_number = 3724 ) AND t4.round_trip_cost is NOT null AND t3.airline_code = "US";

116. and how much does it cost to travel from OAK airport to downtown
P: do you have the fare for traveling from OAK airport to OAKLAND downtown

SELECT DISTINCT t3.ground_fare FROM ground_service AS t3 JOIN airport AS t2 ON t3.airport_code = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t3.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE t2.airport_code = "OAK" AND t1.city_name = "OAKLAND";

117. what is the cheapest COACH fare from DALLAS to DENVER round trip

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t6.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" AND t2.class_type = "COACH" ) AND t5.round_trip_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t6.round_trip_cost ) FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE t5.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t2.class_type = "COACH" );

118. i'd like a nonstop flight from NASHVILLE to ST. LOUIS that gets in around 7pm
P: find a nonstop flight between NASHVILLE and ST. LOUIS arriving in ST. LOUIS around 5pm
P: i need a nonstop flight from NASHVILLE to ST. LOUIS arriving between 1200 and 2000
P: i would like a flight from NASHVILLE to ST. LOUIS that arrives in ST. LOUIS around 6pm and is nonstop
P: what nonstop flights are available from NASHVILLE to ST. LOUIS arriving between 1200 and 2000
P: what flights are there between NASHVILLE and ST. LOUIS which are nonstop and arrive after 1200 and before 2000

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.arrival_time <= 2000 AND t5.arrival_time >= 1200 ) AND t3.city_name = "ST. LOUIS" ) AND t4.city_name = "NASHVILLE" ) AND t5.stops = 0;

120. does YX serve INDIANAPOLIS
P: what are all the flights on YX in and out of INDIANAPOLIS

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM flight AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.from_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" ) ) AND t5.airline_code = "YX";

121. flights from BOSTON 6 13
P: show me all the flights out of BOSTON today

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN days AS t5 ON t4.flight_days = t5.days_code JOIN date_day AS t3 ON t5.day_name = t3.day_name WHERE t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.day_number = 13 AND t3.month_number = 6 AND t3.year = 1991;

122. give me all nonstops from NEW YORK to LAS VEGAS that arrive on a SUNDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t6.day_name = "SATURDAY" ) OR ( t6.day_name = "SUNDAY" AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" ) AND t3.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

123. please book for me a flight on AA from PHILADELPHIA to DALLAS earliest possible time

P: earliest flight on AA from PHILADELPHIA to DALLAS
P: what is the earliest flight that AA has between PHILADELPHIA and DALLAS
P: i would like to book on AA their earliest possible flight from PHILADELPHIA to DALLAS
P: what is the earliest AA flight leaving PHILADELPHIA for DALLAS

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t5.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t1.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t5.airline_code = "AA" );

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code WHERE t5.city_name = "LONG BEACH" AND t4.city_name = "MEMPHIS" AND t1.state_name = "CALIFORNIA" AND t2.state_name = "TENNESSEE";

128. what flights go from BOSTON to ATLANTA before 500 o'clock sunday afternoon
P: list all flights going from BOSTON to ATLANTA before 500 on thursday
P: a listing of all flights from BOSTON to ATLANTA before 500 on thursday
P: all flights from BOSTON to ATLANTA on 5 24 before 500

P: flights from BOSTON to ATLANTA on wednesday before 500

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time < 500 ) AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

129. what flights from ST. PAUL to KANSAS CITY on friday with DINNER served
P: what are the DINNER flights from ST. PAUL to KANSAS CITY on wednesday may twelfth
P: what flights from ST. PAUL to KANSAS CITY on friday with supper served

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN food_service AS t7 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 25 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t7.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t2.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) AND t3.city_name = "ST. PAUL";

130. what flight goes from DENVER to BALTIMORE FIRST class on UA arriving on 5 7

SELECT DISTINCT t7.flight_id FROM days AS t15 JOIN date_day AS t10 ON t15.day_name = t10.day_name JOIN flight AS t7 ON t7.flight_days = t15.days_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t7.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t8 ON t2.fare_id = t8.fare_id JOIN flight_fare AS t12 ON t7.flight_id = t12.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t14 ON t7.to_airport = t14.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t13 ON t7.from_airport = t13.airport_code JOIN fare_basis AS t5 ON t8.fare_basis_code = t5.fare_basis_code JOIN fare_basis AS t4 ON t8.fare_basis_code = t4.fare_basis_code JOIN days AS t16 ON t4.basis_days = t16.days_code JOIN fare AS t9 ON t12.fare_id = t9.fare_id JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t14.city_code JOIN date_day AS t11 ON t1.city_code = t13.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t9.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t13.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t7.departure_time > t7.arrival_time ) AND t10.day_number = 6 AND t10.month_number = 5 AND t10.year = 1991 ) AND t11.day_number = 6 AND t11.month_number = 5 AND t11.year = 1991 AND t5.class_type = "FIRST" ) OR ( ( t10.day_number = 7 AND t10.month_number = 5 AND t10.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t7.departure_time > t7.arrival_time ) ) AND t11.day_number = 7 AND t11.month_number = 5 AND t11.year = 1991 AND t5.class_type = "FIRST" ) ) AND t3.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t6.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t1.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t7.airline_code = "UA";

131. morning flights out of SAN FRANCISCO arriving DENVER afternoon

P: show me the flight that leaves SAN FRANCISCO in the afternoon and arrives in the evening in DENVER
P: i need a flight from SAN FRANCISCO to DENVER leaving in the afternoon and arriving in the evening thank you
P: is there a flight in the afternoon from SAN FRANCISCO that arrives in the evening in DENVER
P: i want a flight from SAN FRANCISCO to DENVER leaving SAN FRANCISCO in the afternoon arriving DENVER around 5 in the afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.arrival_time <= 1730 AND t5.arrival_time >= 1630 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

132. please give me flight schedules from BALTIMORE to PHILADELPHIA
P: show me the flight schedule from BALTIMORE to PHILADELPHIA

SELECT DISTINCT t1.arrival_time , t1.departure_time FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_leg AS t5 ON t2.flight_id = t5.flight_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t5.leg_flight WHERE t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA";

133. what are the nonstop flights from KANSAS CITY to BURBANK arriving on saturday may 22

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "BURBANK" ) AND t3.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

P: i would like a nonstop flight from ST. PETERSBURG to CHARLOTTE leaving in the afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) AND ( t5.stops = 0 ) ) AND t3.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" ) AND t4.city_name = "ST. PETERSBURG";

P: which airline provides BUSINESS class flights

SELECT DISTINCT t5.airline_code FROM fare AS t2 JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t2.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airline AS t5 ON t4.airline_code = t5.airline_code WHERE t3.class_type = "BUSINESS";

141. what is your last trip on 4 23 from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON

P: what 's the latest flight out of ATLANTA that arrives in WASHINGTON next monday
P: what is your last trip from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON on 4 23
P: show me the latest flight on wednesday from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON

P: what is the latest departure from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON on the 23 of 4
P: what is the last flight leaving ATLANTA going to WASHINGTON on friday
P: find me the latest flight leaving ATLANTA 4 23 and arriving in WASHINGTON
P: what is the latest flight leaving ATLANTA for WASHINGTON wednesday
P: what is the latest flight from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON tomorrow
P: what is the last flight from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON this wednesday
P: can you list the latest flights from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON on wednesday
P: what is the latest flight on wednesday going from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" );

143. what is the distance between DALLAS airport and downtown DALLAS

144. show me the flights before 1200 on 2 21 from DENVER to CHICAGO on CO

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time < 1200 ) AND t2.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t1.airline_code = "CO";

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight AS t3 JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t2 ON t3.to_airport = t2.airport_code WHERE ( t1.airport_code = "BOS" AND t2.airport_code = "BWI" ) AND t3.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t3.departure_time ) FROM flight AS t3 JOIN airport AS t2 ON t3.from_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE t2.airport_code = "BOS" AND t1.airport_code = "BWI" );

149. are there any US flights flying into PITTSBURGH between 1200 and 1600 in the afternoon

P: what about the US flights arriving in PITTSBURGH between 1200 and 1600 in the afternoon

150. what are the COACH fares for flights from NEWARK to LOS ANGELES leaving after 1500

151. on tuesday i'd like to find a flight from CLEVELAND to MIAMI that arrives before 1600

P: on friday i need to see all flights that leave CLEVELAND and arrive in MIAMI before 1600

P: i would like information on flights from CLEVELAND to MIAMI on thursday arriving in MIAMI before 1600
P: i want a list of flights from CLEVELAND to MIAMI on thursday that arrive in MIAMI before 1600
P: i need a thursday flight from CLEVELAND to MIAMI arriving in MIAMI before 1600 o'clock
P: what flights depart CLEVELAND on friday and arrive in MIAMI by 1600
P: list flights leaving CLEVELAND on saturday and arriving in MIAMI before 1600

P: i would like to fly from CLEVELAND to MIAMI on saturday and arrive in MIAMI before 1600
P: CLEVELAND to MIAMI on wednesday arriving before 1600

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.arrival_time < 1600 ) AND t2.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t3.city_name = "CLEVELAND";

153. what airplane types fly from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE
P: list number of people that can be carried on each type of plane that flies between PITTSBURGH and BALTIMORE

P: list types of aircraft that fly between PITTSBURGH and BALTIMORE
P: what type of aircraft leaving PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE
P: list types of aircraft that connect PITTSBURGH and BALTIMORE
P: list aircraft types that fly between PITTSBURGH and BALTIMORE
P: list types of planes that fly between PITTSBURGH and BALTIMORE

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE";

158. i'd like to book the cheapest one way flight from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA on 7 20
P: i'd like also to book a one way flight from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA the cheapest one on 7 20

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t3.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t6.day_number = 20 AND t6.month_number = 7 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t5.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name WHERE ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t6.day_number = 20 AND t6.month_number = 7 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t2.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

159. give me the latest flight tomorrow on TW from MILWAUKEE to TACOMA

P: give me the latest TW flight from MILWAUKEE to TACOMA tomorrow

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "TACOMA" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" ) AND t1.airline_code = "TW" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "TACOMA" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" ) AND t1.airline_code = "TW" );

160. i want to leave ATLANTA and arrive in BALTIMORE at 1900 o'clock in the afternoon
