SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t5.arrival_time = 1900 ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA";

161. what is the total schedule for DL 's flights to all airports

SELECT DISTINCT t3.arrival_time , t3.departure_time FROM flight AS t3 JOIN flight_leg AS t4 ON t3.flight_id = t4.leg_flight JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t4.flight_id JOIN airport AS t2 ON t1.to_airport = t2.airport_code WHERE t3.airline_code = "DL";

162. i'd like a nonstop flight from INDIANAPOLIS to SAN DIEGO that serves DINNER what 's available

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "SAN DIEGO" AND t6.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t3.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

163. is there RENTAL CAR service available at TAMPA airport
P: i'll need a RENTAL CAR at the TAMPA airport can you show me what 's available
P: is there an airport RENTAL CAR at the TAMPA airport
P: can i get a RENTAL CAR in TAMPA
P: can i get a RENTAL CAR from TAMPA airport to downtown TAMPA
P: i need to RENTAL CAR at TAMPA

SELECT DISTINCT t4.transport_type FROM airport AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN ground_service AS t4 ON t4.airport_code = t3.airport_code WHERE t2.city_name = "TAMPA" AND t4.transport_type = "RENTAL CAR";

164. show me the type of aircraft that CP uses

SELECT DISTINCT t2.basic_type FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t2 ON t1.aircraft_code = t2.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence WHERE t3.airline_code = "CP";

165. i need a flight from PHOENIX ARIZONA to ST. PAUL MINNESOTA leaving this sunday
P: may i have a listing of flight numbers from PHOENIX ARIZONA to ST. PAUL MINNESOTA on monday
P: i want a flight from PHOENIX ARIZONA to ST. PAUL MINNESOTA that leaves sunday
P: may i have a listing of flights from PHOENIX ARIZONA to ST. PAUL MINNESOTA on wednesday
P: i would like a flight that leaves on sunday from PHOENIX ARIZONA to ST. PAUL MINNESOTA
P: what are the flights from PHOENIX ARIZONA to ST. PAUL MINNESOTA on tuesday

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t3.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name WHERE ( t4.city_name = "ST. PAUL" AND t6.day_number = 22 AND t6.month_number = 3 AND t6.year = 1991 AND t2.state_name = "MINNESOTA" ) AND t5.city_name = "PHOENIX" AND t1.state_name = "ARIZONA";

166. show me all flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE which arrive before 1000 o'clock am on wednesday
P: show me all flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE which arrive before 1000 on wednesday
P: flight from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE arriving before 1000 on saturday
P: show me all flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE which arrive in BALTIMORE before 1000 o'clock pm on saturday
P: i would like information on any flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE arriving in BALTIMORE before 1000 tuesday morning
P: show me all flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE which arrive in BALTIMORE before 1000 o'clock am tomorrow
P: show me all flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE which arrive in BALTIMORE wednesday before 1000
P: i would like information on flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE arriving in BALTIMORE before 1000 on thursday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) AND t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1000 ) AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

167. i would like to fly to BALTIMORE for under 300 dollars please show me the airfares between DALLAS and BALTIMORE
P: show me fares less than 300 dollars for flights from DALLAS to BALTIMORE
P: show me fares from DALLAS to BALTIMORE that cost less than 300 dollars

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE t5.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t4.one_direction_cost < 300;

168. please list the cheapest flights from DALLAS to BALTIMORE arriving on 5 7
P: please list the cheapest flight from DALLAS to BALTIMORE arriving on 5 7

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t3.arrival_time < 41 OR t3.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t3.departure_time > t3.arrival_time ) AND t6.day_number = 6 AND t6.month_number = 5 AND t6.year = 1991 ) OR ( t6.day_number = 7 AND t6.month_number = 5 AND t6.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t3.arrival_time < 41 OR t3.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t3.departure_time > t3.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t2.arrival_time < 41 OR t2.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t2.departure_time > t2.arrival_time ) AND t6.day_number = 6 AND t6.month_number = 5 AND t6.year = 1991 ) OR ( t6.day_number = 7 AND t6.month_number = 5 AND t6.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t2.arrival_time < 41 OR t2.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t2.departure_time > t2.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

169. i want to fly from BOSTON to ORLANDO with a stop in NEW YORK on a BREAKFAST flight
P: i need a flight from BOSTON to ORLANDO stopping in NEW YORK the flight should also serve BREAKFAST
P: i'd like a flight from BOSTON to ORLANDO stopping in NEW YORK and serving BREAKFAST what 's available
P: on a BREAKFAST flight from BOSTON to ORLANDO via NEW YORK
P: i would like to find a flight that goes from BOSTON to ORLANDO making a stop in NEW YORK and a flight that serves BREAKFAST
P: i'm looking for a flight from BOSTON to ORLANDO that stops in NEW YORK hopefully a BREAKFAST flight how can i find that out
P: i would like to find a flight that goes from BOSTON to ORLANDO i would like it to have a stop in NEW YORK and i would like a flight that serves BREAKFAST

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t8 ON t8.stop_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t8.flight_id JOIN food_service AS t9 ON t9.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "NEW YORK" AND t9.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t3.city_name = "ORLANDO" ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

P: what does code Q mean

P: DL flights with stops in ATLANTA
P: DL stopping in ATLANTA
P: DL flights stopping in ATLANTA

172. give me all flights from MEMPHIS to LAS VEGAS that arrive on a SUNDAY
P: what're the flights from MEMPHIS to LAS VEGAS that arrive on a SUNDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t6.day_name = "SATURDAY" ) OR ( t6.day_name = "SUNDAY" AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" ) AND t3.city_name = "MEMPHIS";

173. which airlines fly into and out of DENVER
P: what airlines leave from DENVER
P: what airlines flies out of DENVER

P: give me a list of airlines in DENVER
P: which airlines serve DENVER
P: what airlines fly into DENVER
P: what airlines go to DENVER
P: what airlines service DENVER airport
P: list the airlines with flights to or from DENVER

SELECT DISTINCT t4.airline_code FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airline AS t4 ON t3.airline_code = t4.airline_code WHERE t2.city_name = "DENVER";

174. how many flights does CO have with a class of service code F

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t3.flight_id ) FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id WHERE t2.fare_basis_code = "F" AND t3.airline_code = "CO";

175. what 's the ground transportation from OAKLAND to SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t3.transport_type FROM ground_service AS t3 JOIN city AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t3.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t1.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO";

176. i'd like to leave DENVER in the afternoon and arrive in SAN FRANCISCO at 1700
P: i would like a flight between DENVER and SAN FRANCISCO leaving from DENVER in the afternoon and arriving at 1700

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t5.arrival_time = 1700 ) AND t4.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

177. show me all flights both direct and connecting to either SAN FRANCISCO or OAKLAND from BOSTON that arrive before 1400

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) OR ( t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1400 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

178. can you please tell me the type of aircraft used flying from ATLANTA to DENVER on EA flight 825 leaving at 555
P: EA flight 825 from ATLANTA to DENVER leaving at 555 what type of aircraft is used on that flight
P: on EA flight 825 flying from ATLANTA to DENVER can you tell me what type of aircraft is used on a flight when it leaves at 555

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( ( t2.departure_time = 555 AND t2.flight_number = 825 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t2.airline_code = "EA";

179. show me all flights from BOSTON to OAKLAND on UA departing at 838
P: please show me any UA flights including connections between BOSTON and OAKLAND at 838 in the evening
P: show me all the UA flights from BOSTON to OAKLAND that leave at 838

P: please list UA flights between BOSTON and OAKLAND departing at 838
P: i want to go from BOSTON to OAKLAND on UA and leave at 838 which flight should i take

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t5.departure_time = 838 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.airline_code = "UA";

180. find travel arrangements for a round trip flight from DALLAS to PITTSBURGH arriving after 2000

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.round_trip_cost is NOT null AND t3.arrival_time > 2000 ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS";

181. what flights are available with Q fares from BOSTON to PITTSBURGH

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id WHERE ( t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t2.fare_basis_code = "Q" ) AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON";

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t7.day_name = "WEDNESDAY" AND t6.day_name = "THURSDAY" ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

185. which airline has the most FIRST class flights
P: how many flights does each airline have with FIRST class service
P: which airline has more FIRST class flights than any other airline

SELECT DISTINCT COUNT ( * ) , t4.airline_code FROM fare AS t2 JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t2.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id WHERE t3.class_type = "FIRST" GROUP BY t4.airline_code;

186. does AA flight from LONG BEACH to ST. LOUIS stopping in DALLAS serve LUNCH

LOUIS" ) AND t4.city_name = "LONG BEACH" ) AND t1.airline_code = "AA";

LOUIS" AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t6.city_name = "TAMPA";

200. i'd like to fly from CLEVELAND to INDIANAPOLIS tomorrow morning as early as possible what 's available

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.city_name = "CLEVELAND" AND t2.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" ) AND ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) ) AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "CLEVELAND" AND t2.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" ) AND ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) ) AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 );

203. what is the last flight out of PITTSBURGH to BOSTON in the evening on TUESDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t6.day_name = "TUESDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t6.day_name = "TUESDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 );

209. list all AA flights from PHOENIX to MILWAUKEE which arrive on wednesday after 1600

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time > 1600 ) AND t2.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" ) AND t3.city_name = "PHOENIX" ) AND t1.airline_code = "AA";

210. okay i would like to know the type of aircraft used on a flight from CLEVELAND to DALLAS please

SELECT DISTINCT t5.basic_type FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE t4.city_name = "CLEVELAND" AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS";

213. find travel arrangements for a round trip flight from BALTIMORE to PITTSBURGH after 2000 o'clock pm before 2200 o'clock pm

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.round_trip_cost is NOT null AND t3.departure_time < 2200 ) AND t3.departure_time > 2000 ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t5.city_name = "BALTIMORE";

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t1.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 );

220. what is the earliest flight arriving in SALT LAKE CITY from OAKLAND on friday
P: what is the first flight arriving in SALT LAKE CITY from OAKLAND friday
P: get first flight from OAKLAND to SALT LAKE CITY on thursday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY" ) AND t3.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t1.arrival_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.arrival_time ) FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY" ) AND t3.city_name = "OAKLAND" );

221. can you list all nonstop flights between ST. PETERSBURG and CHARLOTTE that leave in the afternoon and arrive soon after 1700

PETERSBURG" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) AND t5.stops = 0;

225. can i fly from ST. PAUL to SAN JOSE HOUSTON
P: which flights are between ST. PAUL and SAN JOSE HOUSTON
P: hi i'm calling from ST. PAUL i'd like to make a flight to either SAN JOSE or HOUSTON
P: i'm flying from ST. PAUL to the bay area
P: i'm interested in a flight from ST. PAUL to SAN JOSE and i'm also interested in going to HOUSTON
P: list the flights from ST. PAUL to SAN JOSE and from ST. PAUL to HOUSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN JOSE" ) OR ( t2.city_name = "HOUSTON" ) ) AND t4.city_name = "ST. PAUL";

226. which are the flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE or WASHINGTON

228. economy fares NEW YORK to MIAMI round trip

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t6.city_name = "NEW YORK" AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t2.economy = "YES" ) AND t5.round_trip_cost is NOT null;

229. show me city served both by NX and CP

SELECT DISTINCT t5.city_code FROM airport AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.airport_code = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t2 ON t2.airport_code = t7.airport_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t2.airport_code WHERE t3.airline_code = "NX" AND t4.airline_code = "CP";

230. i would like to fly from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA on US at the latest time possible in the evening

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.airline_code = "US" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t1.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.airline_code = "US" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 );

232. list all AA flights from MIAMI to CHICAGO that arrive in CHICAGO between 1630 and 1730
P: show me all the AA flights from MIAMI to CHICAGO that arrive around 11am
P: i'm trying to find the flight number from a flight from MIAMI to CHICAGO on AA and it arrives around 10pm
P: i'd like to find a AA flight from MIAMI to CHICAGO that arrives around 10 o'clock in the evening
P: what are the flights from MIAMI to CHICAGO on AA that arrive around 10pm
P: i want to fly from MIAMI to CHICAGO on AA and arrive at around 5 o'clock in the afternoon show me all flights
P: i need a flight on AA from MIAMI to CHICAGO that arrives around 5pm
P: i'd like to fly from MIAMI to CHICAGO on on AA arriving around 5pm

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.arrival_time <= 1730 AND t5.arrival_time >= 1630 ) AND t3.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t4.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t5.airline_code = "AA";

233. is there a UA flight from MIAMI to WASHINGTON arriving around noon

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.arrival_time <= 1230 AND t5.arrival_time >= 1130 ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t3.state_code = "DC" ) AND t4.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t5.airline_code = "UA";

234. what is the most expensive flight from BOSTON to DALLAS round trip

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t5.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t2.round_trip_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.round_trip_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

235. please list all flights into DENVER before 1200 on UA and NW

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE ( ( t3.airline_code = "NW" ) OR ( t3.airline_code = "UA" ) ) AND ( t2.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.arrival_time < 1200 );

236. how many airlines have flights with service class YN

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t4.airline_code ) FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airline AS t4 ON t3.airline_code = t4.airline_code WHERE t2.fare_basis_code = "YN";

237. what're the cheapest nonstop flights from NEW YORK to MIAMI one way

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t5.city_name = "NEW YORK" AND t4.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t3.stops = 0 ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "NEW YORK" AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t2.stops = 0 ) AND t2.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

238. US 269 leaving BOSTON at 1628 what is the arrival time in BALTIMORE

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.departure_time = 1628 AND t5.flight_number = 269 ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.airline_code = "US";

239. give me the flights from NEW YORK to LAS VEGAS on sunday and the flights from MEMPHIS to LAS VEGAS on sunday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t1.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" AND t5.day_number = 27 AND t5.month_number = 8 AND t5.year = 1991 ) AND ( ( t4.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "MEMPHIS" ) );

242. what is the fare from BOSTON to WASHINGTON FIRST class one way
P: what is the fare from BOSTON to WASHINGTON on FIRST one way
P: how much does it cost to fly one way from BOSTON to WASHINGTON FIRST class

SELECT DISTINCT t3.fare_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN fare AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN fare_basis AS t1 ON t3.fare_basis_code = t1.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t3.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t1.class_type = "FIRST";

PAUL";

246. what flights are available from BOSTON to washington dc late the 25 or early the 26

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 2400 AND t1.departure_time >= 2000 ) AND t4.day_number = 25 AND t4.month_number = 11 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 11 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time <= 1000 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO";

247. yes on the DL flight leaving SAN FRANCISCO at 1425 arriving PHILADELPHIA 2358 what type of equipment is used on that flight

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( ( t2.arrival_time = 2358 AND t2.departure_time = 1425 ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t2.airline_code = "DL";

249. what are the flights from DALLAS to BOSTON for tomorrow night or evening

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) OR ( t1.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759 ) ) AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS";

250. does any airline have an afternoon flight from BOSTON to DENVER

251. where does flight DL 838 from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA stop
P: i would like to know if i fly on DL flight number 838 from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA if i will stop enroute at another city
P: what stops does DL 838 make from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA

SELECT DISTINCT t6.stop_airport FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN flight_stop AS t6 ON t1.flight_id = t6.flight_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t1.flight_number = 838 ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t1.airline_code = "DL";

252. what flights are available on DL from DALLAS to ATLANTA on monday morning

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.airline_code = "DL" ) AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200;

253. what is the earliest BREAKFAST flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE
P: what is the first flight that travels from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE that serves BREAKFAST
P: what is the first flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE that serves BREAKFAST
P: find me the earliest flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE that serves BREAKFAST
P: find the earliest BREAKFAST flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE
P: i need the earliest flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE that serves BREAKFAST
P: what is the earliest flight between ATLANTA and BALTIMORE that serves BREAKFAST
P: show me the earliest flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE that serves a BREAKFAST
P: please list the earliest BREAKFAST flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE
P: find the earliest flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE that serves BREAKFAST
P: what is the first flight that goes from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE that serves BREAKFAST

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t6.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t6.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" );

255. what flights do you have from NEWARK NEW JERSEY to ONTARIO CALIFORNIA that connect in PHOENIX

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t10 ON t10.stop_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t10.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t6.state_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.connections > 0 ) AND t4.city_name = "PHOENIX" ) AND t5.city_name = "ONTARIO" AND t2.state_name = "CALIFORNIA" ) AND t6.city_name = "NEWARK" AND t1.state_name = "NEW JERSEY";

256. i am interested in a flight from CINCINNATI to BURBANK the flight should be AA and leave in the afternoon i need to know the aircraft and flight number

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code , t2.flight_number FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "CINCINNATI" AND t3.city_name = "BURBANK" ) AND t2.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

257. what flights does US have from MIAMI to CLEVELAND after 1200 o'clock
P: is there a flight from MIAMI to CLEVELAND on US leaving after 1200 o'clock in the afternoon
P: what US flights from MIAMI to CLEVELAND depart MIAMI after 1200 on wednesday
P: list all flights on US from MIAMI to CLEVELAND which depart after 1200
P: all right what US flights leave from MIAMI to CLEVELAND after 1200 in the afternoon
P: i'd like a flight on US from MIAMI to CLEVELAND that leaves after 1200
P: which US flights depart from MIAMI heading toward CLEVELAND after 1200
P: what flights does US have from MIAMI to CLEVELAND after 1200
P: show flights leaving MIAMI to CLEVELAND on US that leave after 1200

258. what flights leave PITTSBURGH and arrive in LOS ANGELES after 1700 on thursday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time > 1700 ) AND t2.city_name = "LOS ANGELES" ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

259. i need a flight from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA next monday
P: on monday i'd like to travel from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA
P: may i have a listing of flights on monday from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA please
P: may i have a listing of flights from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA on tuesday
P: list all the flights from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA that leave next monday
P: do you have a flight from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA next monday
P: i need to fly from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA next monday
P: may i have a listing of flights from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA on wednesday
P: tell me about flights from ATLANTA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA leaving on monday and arriving in CHARLOTTE

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t3.state_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t2.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t8.day_name = t5.day_name WHERE ( t3.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" AND t5.day_number = 21 AND t5.month_number = 2 AND t5.year = 1991 AND t1.state_name = "NORTH CAROLINA" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA";

260. please list any flight available leaving OAKLAND california tuesday arriving PHILADELPHIA wednesday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 3 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t3.city_name = "OAKLAND";

262. tell me about flights leaving from ATLANTA and going to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA next monday i need to know about flights that arrive in CHARLOTTE between 1615 and 1730

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t8.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t3.state_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t2.arrival_time <= 1730 AND t2.arrival_time >= 1615 ) AND NOT ( ( t2.arrival_time <= 41 OR t2.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t2.departure_time > t2.arrival_time ) ) AND t5.day_number = 21 AND t5.month_number = 2 AND t5.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" AND t1.state_name = "NORTH CAROLINA" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA";

265. i want to know the time of the latest flight i can take from WASHINGTON to SAN FRANCISCO where i can get a DINNER meal

SELECT DISTINCT t1.departure_time FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t6.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t6.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" );

266. does any airline offer DC10 service between DENVER and BOSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t8.airline_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airline AS t8 ON t2.airline_code = t8.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( t5.basic_type = "DC10" AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t4.city_name = "DENVER";

PAUL" AND t5.arrival_time <= 1700 ) AND t4.city_name = "KANSAS CITY";

270. of all airlines which airline has the most arrivals in ATLANTA
P: which airline has the most arrivals in ATLANTA

SELECT DISTINCT COUNT ( * ) , t3.airline_code FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" GROUP BY t3.airline_code;

271. what flights from LOS ANGELES to PITTSBURGH arrive next saturday before 1500
P: what flights from LOS ANGELES to PITTSBURGH arriving before 1500 on monday
P: i want a flight from LOS ANGELES to PITTSBURGH that arrives before 1500 on tuesday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 3 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 3 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1500 ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t3.city_name = "LOS ANGELES";

272. please show me airlines with round trip flights from BOSTON to DENVER stop PHILADELPHIA

SELECT DISTINCT t11.airline_code FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t10 ON t10.stop_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t10.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airline AS t11 ON t3.airline_code = t11.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t5.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t6.city_name = "BOSTON";

273. round trip fares from PITTSBURGH to PHILADELPHIA less than 1000 dollars

P: round trip air fares from PITTSBURGH to PHILADELPHIA less than 1000 dollars
P: round trip fare from PITTSBURGH to PHILADELPHIA less than 1000 dollars

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE ( t5.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t4.round_trip_cost < 1000 ) AND t4.round_trip_cost is NOT null;

P: i'd like a CO flight from LAS VEGAS to NEW YORK nonstop

275. i would like the flights available from BOSTON to DENVER arriving in DENVER on 800 o'clock wednesday morning on or by 800 o'clock wednesday morning
P: i would like information on flights from BOSTON to DENVER arriving in DENVER on tuesday morning
P: i would like to know the flights available from BOSTON to DENVER arriving in DENVER by 800 o'clock wednesday morning

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time <= 800 ) AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

281. please give me direct morning flights from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA

286. what is the least expensive BUSINESS class flight between BOSTON and SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t6.flight_id FROM city AS t8 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t8.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight AS t6 ON t6.from_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t10 ON t6.to_airport = t10.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t6.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t4 ON t2.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t4.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t7 ON t7.city_code = t10.city_code , fare AS t5 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t8.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t7.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.class_type = "BUSINESS" ) AND t5.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t6.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t7 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t7.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t5.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t10 ON t5.flight_id = t10.flight_id JOIN flight_fare AS t4 ON t5.flight_id = t4.flight_id JOIN fare AS t6 ON t10.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN fare AS t2 ON t4.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t2.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code WHERE t7.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t1.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t3.class_type = "BUSINESS" ) AND t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id AND t6.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

287. give me the cheapest round trip flight from ATLANTA to PITTSBURGH
P: list the cheapest round trip flights from ATLANTA to PITTSBURGH
P: what are the cheapest round trip flights from ATLANTA to PITTSBURGH
P: show me the cheapest round trips from ATLANTA to PITTSBURGH
P: what is the cheapest way to travel round trip from ATLANTA to PITTSBURGH
P: what is the cheapest round trip flight from ATLANTA to PITTSBURGH
P: can you show me the cheapest round trip flights between ATLANTA and PITTSBURGH
P: show me the cheapest flights round trip from ATLANTA to PITTSBURGH

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t5.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t2.round_trip_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.round_trip_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

291. what is the schedule of ground transportation from the airport in PITTSBURGH into downtown
P: can i see ground transportation from PITTSBURGH airport to downtown
P: is there ground transportation from the airport in PITTSBURGH to downtown
P: how do i get from PITTSBURGH airport to downtown PITTSBURGH
P: how can i get from the PITTSBURGH airport to downtown
P: what ground transportation is there from the airport in PITTSBURGH to downtown
P: what is the schedule of ground transportation from PITTSBURGH airport into downtown
P: what transportation is available from the PITTSBURGH airport to downtown
P: what ground transportation is available from PITTSBURGH to downtown
P: what ground transportation is available from the PITTSBURGH airport to the town

SELECT DISTINCT t5.transport_type FROM airport AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN ground_service AS t5 ON t5.airport_code = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t5.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

292. are there any TURBOPROP flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE on 12 17

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( t5.propulsion = "TURBOPROP" AND t6.day_number = 17 AND t6.month_number = 12 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

293. from KANSAS CITY to SALT LAKE CITY on DL arrive around 8pm tomorrow

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND ( t1.arrival_time <= 2030 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1930 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY" ) AND t3.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) AND t1.airline_code = "DL";

295. is there a flight between SAN FRANCISCO and BOSTON with a stopover in DALLAS FORT WORTH on DL

P: i'd like to fly from SAN FRANCISCO to BOSTON with a stopover in DALLAS FORT WORTH and i want to fly on DL

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t10 ON t10.stop_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_stop AS t11 ON t1.flight_id = t10.flight_id JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t11.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t11.stop_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t9.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t1.airline_code = "DL";

298. could you give me the schedule of flights for AA and DL to DFW on 8 15

SELECT DISTINCT t2.arrival_time , t2.departure_time FROM days AS t6 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t6.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN flight_leg AS t5 ON t3.flight_id = t5.flight_id JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_id = t5.leg_flight WHERE ( ( ( t3.airline_code = "AA" ) OR ( t3.airline_code = "DL" ) ) AND t4.day_number = 15 AND t4.month_number = 8 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.airport_code = "DFW";

299. i would like a list of round trip flights between INDIANAPOLIS and ORLANDO FLORIDA for the 27 and the 28 of 12

SELECT DISTINCT t7.flight_id FROM days AS t15 JOIN date_day AS t11 ON t15.day_name = t11.day_name JOIN flight AS t7 ON t7.flight_days = t15.days_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t7.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t8 ON t2.fare_id = t8.fare_id JOIN flight_fare AS t3 ON t7.flight_id = t3.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t13 ON t7.to_airport = t13.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t12 ON t7.from_airport = t12.airport_code JOIN fare_basis AS t4 ON t8.fare_basis_code = t4.fare_basis_code JOIN days AS t14 ON t4.basis_days = t14.days_code JOIN fare AS t9 ON t3.fare_id = t9.fare_id JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t13.city_code JOIN state AS t5 ON t5.state_code = t6.state_code JOIN date_day AS t10 ON t1.city_code = t12.city_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t12.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t11.day_number = 27 AND t11.month_number = 12 AND t11.year = 1991 AND t10.day_number = 27 AND t10.month_number = 12 AND t10.year = 1991 AND t8.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) OR ( t11.day_number = 28 AND t11.month_number = 12 AND t11.year = 1991 AND t10.day_number = 28 AND t10.month_number = 12 AND t10.year = 1991 AND t8.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) ) AND t9.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t6.city_name = "ORLANDO" AND t5.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t1.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS";

300. what is the number of FIRST class flights on DL
P: how many flights does DL have with FIRST class
P: how many FIRST class flights are provided by DL
P: how many flights does DL have in FIRST class
P: how many FIRST class flights does DL have

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t4.flight_id ) FROM fare AS t2 JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t2.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id WHERE t3.class_type = "FIRST" AND t4.airline_code = "DL";

302. list all nonstop flights on wednesday from BALTIMORE to NEWARK before 1200

P: list all nonstop flights from BALTIMORE to NEWARK before 1200 on tuesday
P: list nonstop flights from BALTIMORE to NEWARK on wednesday before 1200

303. list nonstop flights on sunday from NEW YORK to LAS VEGAS and list nonstop flights on sunday from MEMPHIS to LAS VEGAS
P: list all flights from NEW YORK to LAS VEGAS that fly nonstop on sunday and list flights from MEMPHIS to LAS VEGAS that fly nonstop on sunday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t1.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" AND t5.day_number = 27 AND t5.month_number = 8 AND t5.year = 1991 ) AND ( ( t4.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "MEMPHIS" ) ) ) AND t1.stops = 0;

307. i would like to find flights from COLUMBUS to MINNEAPOLIS on monday june fourteenth early in the morning or in the evening sunday june thirteenth thank you

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 800 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "MINNEAPOLIS" ) AND t3.city_name = "COLUMBUS";

309. how much does a FIRST class round trip ticket from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO on UA cost

P: what is the round trip FIRST fare on UA from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN food_service AS t7 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND ( t1.airline_code = "CO" ) ) AND t2.city_name = "SEATTLE" ) AND t3.city_name = "CHICAGO";

311. give me the flights from CHICAGO to ST. PAUL that have meals on CO saturday morning
P: give me the flights from CHICAGO to ST. PAUL on CO that have meals early saturday morning
P: give me a combination of CO flights from CHICAGO to ST. PAUL that have meals early saturday morning
P: give me the saturday morning flights on CO that have meals from CHICAGO to ST. PAUL
P: give me the saturday morning flights from CHICAGO to ST. PAUL on CO that have meals

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE ( ( ( ( ( flight_days IN ( SELECT days_code FROM days WHERE day_name IN ( SELECT day_name FROM date_day WHERE day_number = 26 AND month_number = 7 AND year = 1991 ) ) AND meal_code IN ( SELECT meal_code FROM food_service ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "ST. PAUL" ) ) ) AND from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "CHICAGO" ) ) ) AND departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND airline_code = "CO" );

312. where is GENERAL MITCHELL INTERNATIONAL airport
P: where is GENERAL MITCHELL INTERNATIONAL located

SELECT DISTINCT t2.city_code FROM airport AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE t3.airport_name LIKE "GENERAL MITCHELL INTERNATIONAL";

313. which flight is a one way fare at 329 dollars from DENVER to PITTSBURGH

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id WHERE ( t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t2.one_direction_cost = 329 AND t2.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t5.city_name = "DENVER";

314. show me the flights from NEWARK NEW JERSEY to ONT next saturday

315. what airline besides CONTINENTAL AIRLINES flies between BOSTON and DENVER

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" AND NOT ( t6.airline_name LIKE "CONTINENTAL AIRLINES" );

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM days AS t10 JOIN date_day AS t7 ON t10.day_name = t7.day_name JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_days = t10.days_code JOIN days AS t11 ON t4.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t4.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t4.from_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t4.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t2.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN date_day AS t8 ON t11.day_name = t8.day_name WHERE ( t1.airport_code = "DEN" AND t7.day_number = 27 AND t7.month_number = 8 AND t7.year = 1991 ) AND t6.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t8.day_number = 27 AND t8.month_number = 8 AND t8.year = 1991;

319. i am interested in booking an early flight from DALLAS into HOUSTON and returning in the late evening
P: i am interested in booking an early morning flight from DALLAS into HOUSTON and returning in the late evening

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.departure_time <= 2200 AND t5.departure_time >= 2000 ) AND t3.city_name = "HOUSTON" ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" ) OR ( ( ( t5.departure_time <= 0 AND t5.departure_time >= 800 ) AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t4.city_name = "HOUSTON" );

321. show me the flights from MILWAUKEE to ORLANDO late night on tuesday

P: give me information on flights from MILWAUKEE to ORLANDO on wednesday after 1200 and thursday before 1200
P: i want information on flights from MILWAUKEE to ORLANDO i want to leave after 1200 on wednesday or before 1200 on thursday
P: show me all the flights from MILWAUKEE to ORLANDO that leave after 1200 on wednesday and before 1200 on thursday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time < 1200 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time > 1200 ) ) AND t3.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" AND t2.city_name = "ORLANDO";

326. do you have a flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE nonstop on a BOEING 757 arriving BALTIMORE around 7pm
P: could you please find me a nonstop flight from ATLANTA to BALTIMORE on a BOEING 757 arriving at 7pm

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t2.arrival_time <= 1930 AND t2.arrival_time >= 1830 ) AND t5.basic_type = "757" AND t5.manufacturer = "BOEING" ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t2.stops = 0;

LOUIS" ) ) );

332. what is the cost of RENTAL CAR service in DENVER

333. are there any flights from BOSTON to OAKLAND that stop

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t6 ON t1.flight_id = t6.flight_id WHERE ( t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

334. what 's the cheapest of the DALLAS to ATLANTA flights which are after 1400 in the afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.departure_time > 1400 ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t2.departure_time > 1400 ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

335. does DL aircraft fly DC10

SELECT DISTINCT t2.aircraft_code FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t2 ON t1.aircraft_code = t2.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence WHERE t2.basic_type = "DC10" AND t3.airline_code = "DL";

337. show me the cheapest flight from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA on wednesday which leaves before 1200 and serves BREAKFAST

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM food_service AS t9 JOIN flight AS t3 ON t9.meal_code = t3.meal_code JOIN days AS t10 ON t3.flight_days = t10.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t10.day_name = t6.day_name , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( ( ( t3.departure_time < 1200 AND t9.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t6.day_number = 23 AND t6.month_number = 4 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM food_service AS t10 JOIN flight AS t2 ON t10.meal_code = t2.meal_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.departure_time < 1200 AND t10.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t6.day_number = 23 AND t6.month_number = 4 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

342. what planes does DL use
P: what kinds of planes are used by DL airlines
P: what kinds of planes are used by DL
P: what is the seating capacity of the various airplanes that DL uses
P: what planes are used by DL
P: what types of aircraft does DL fly

SELECT DISTINCT t2.aircraft_code FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t2 ON t1.aircraft_code = t2.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence WHERE t3.airline_code = "DL";

343. show me ground transportation information for BOS
P: what ground transportation is available from the BOS airport
P: what types of ground transportation are there to BOS airport
P: what type of ground transportation is available at BOS airport
P: is there ground transportation in BOS from the airport

SELECT DISTINCT t2.transport_type FROM ground_service AS t2 JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.airport_code = t1.airport_code WHERE t1.airport_code = "BOS";

344. show me all flights from PHILADELPHIA to BOSTON on saturday which serve a meal and arrive in BOSTON before 1200
P: show me all flights from PHILADELPHIA to BOSTON on monday which serve a meal and arrive before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM food_service AS t7 JOIN flight AS t1 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 1200 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA";

345. what is the most expensive flight from DALLAS to BALTIMORE

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t5.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

346. what flights leave SAN FRANCISCO on monday night and arrive at ATLANTA later in the evening

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time <= 2400 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1800 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t1.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759;

347. list the number of flights arriving in DALLAS FORT WORTH from BOSTON before 1200

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t1.flight_id ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1200 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

348. what flights leave CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA and arrive in PHOENIX ARIZONA on monday before 1600
P: on monday i would like to travel from CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA to PHOENIX ARIZONA i would like to arrive in PHOENIX before 1600

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code WHERE ( ( t6.day_number = 21 AND t6.month_number = 2 AND t6.year = 1991 AND t3.arrival_time < 1600 ) AND t4.city_name = "PHOENIX" AND t2.state_name = "ARIZONA" ) AND t5.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" AND t1.state_name = "NORTH CAROLINA";

350. what flights are there from NASHVILLE to HOUSTON tomorrow evening that serve DINNER
P: i'd like a flight tomorrow evening from NASHVILLE to HOUSTON that includes DINNER for tomorrow
P: i'd like a flight tomorrow late from NASHVILLE to HOUSTON with DINNER please

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN food_service AS t7 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 2400 AND t1.departure_time >= 2000 ) AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time <= 300 AND t1.departure_time >= 0 ) ) AND t7.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t2.city_name = "HOUSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "NASHVILLE";

P: wednesday morning flights between BALTIMORE and NEWARK NEW JERSEY

355. i want to fly from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO next wednesday arriving in the evening and returning the next day

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time <= 2200 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1800 ) AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t3.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) OR ( ( t2.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "CHICAGO" );

356. i would like the time of all flights from DENVER to OAKLAND on sunday
P: what time are the flights leaving from DENVER to OAKLAND on 4 23
P: what are the times that you have planes leaving from DENVER going to OAKLAND on 4 23
P: what times on wednesday could i take a plane from DENVER to OAKLAND

SELECT DISTINCT t1.departure_time FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER";
