359. what is the total seating capacity of all aircraft of AA

SELECT DISTINCT t2.aircraft_code , t2.capacity FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t2 ON t1.aircraft_code = t2.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence WHERE t3.airline_code = "AA";

360. what is the cost of a BUSINESS class ticket going from BOSTON to DALLAS leaving 7 1

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN fare_basis AS t1 ON t4.fare_basis_code = t1.fare_basis_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t4.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t1.basis_days = t9.days_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t6.day_number = 1 AND t6.month_number = 7 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t2.class_type = "BUSINESS";

361. list nonstop flights from BOSTON to WASHINGTON which arrive after 1600
P: what nonstop flights between BOSTON and WASHINGTON arrive after 1600 o'clock pm

363. what CO flights from DENVER to CHICAGO arrive at CHICAGO before 1200 on saturday
P: list all flights on CO leaving DENVER and arriving at CHICAGO on monday before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1200 ) AND t2.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t1.airline_code = "CO";

368. now i need flights leaving from PITTSBURGH and arriving in PHILADELPHIA on wednesday morning

P: list the shortest flight from SAN JOSE to HOUSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "SAN JOSE" AND t3.city_name = "HOUSTON" ) AND t5.time_elapsed = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.time_elapsed ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE t2.city_name = "SAN JOSE" AND t1.city_name = "HOUSTON" );

373. i need a flight from TAMPA FLORIDA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA leaving in the afternoon on tuesday
P: i would like to book an early morning flight from TAMPA FLORIDA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA on 4 6

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t3.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" AND t6.day_number = 6 AND t6.month_number = 4 AND t6.year = 1991 AND t2.state_name = "NORTH CAROLINA" ) AND t5.city_name = "TAMPA" AND t1.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t3.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 800;

374. where is MCO

SELECT DISTINCT airport_location FROM airport WHERE airport_code = "MCO";

375. i need a listing of flights from ST. PETERSBURG FLORIDA to TACOMA WASHINGTON leaving tomorrow and i would like to have a stopover in MILWAUKEE please

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t10 ON t4.city_code = t10.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t11 ON t11.stop_airport = t10.airport_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t11.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t3.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN days AS t12 ON t3.flight_days = t12.days_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t6.state_code JOIN date_day AS t7 ON t12.day_name = t7.day_name WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" AND t7.day_number = 20 AND t7.month_number = 1 AND t7.year = 1991 ) AND t5.city_name = "TACOMA" AND t2.state_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t6.city_name = "ST. PETERSBURG" AND t1.state_name = "FLORIDA";

376. do you have an early morning direct flight from PHILADELPHIA to PITTSBURGH

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t5.connections = 0 ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 800;

377. i want to fly from DETROIT to ST. PETERSBURG on NW and leave around 9am tell me what aircraft are used by this flight and tell me the flight number

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code , t2.flight_number FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( ( t2.departure_time <= 930 AND t2.departure_time >= 830 ) AND t3.city_name = "ST. PETERSBURG" ) AND t4.city_name = "DETROIT" ) AND t2.airline_code = "NW";

378. i'd like to travel from BOSTON to BALTIMORE on us air 269 please tell me the times

SELECT DISTINCT t5.arrival_time , t5.departure_time FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t5.flight_number = 269 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

379. how many flights has CO into and out of ATLANTA

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t5.flight_id ) FROM flight AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) ) AND t5.airline_code = "CO";

380. list all flights from CHICAGO to SEATTLE on CO which depart on saturday before 1200 and include a meal

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM food_service AS t7 JOIN flight AS t1 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time < 1200 ) AND t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "SEATTLE" ) AND t3.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t1.airline_code = "CO";

381. how much does it cost to go from downtown to logan airport
P: how much is the ground transportation between ATLANTA and downtown

SELECT DISTINCT t5.ground_fare FROM airport AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN ground_service AS t5 ON t5.airport_code = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t5.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA";

382. are there any other cities that i can fly from BOSTON to DALLAS through that i can get a flight earlier than 1017 in the morning

SELECT DISTINCT t4.city_code FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_stop AS t8 ON t1.flight_id = t8.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t8.stop_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t1.departure_time < 1017 ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

383. shortest morning flights from TAMPA to CINCINNATI
P: shortest evening flight from TAMPA to CINCINNATI

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "TAMPA" AND t3.city_name = "CINCINNATI" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t5.time_elapsed = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.time_elapsed ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "TAMPA" AND t1.city_name = "CINCINNATI" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 );

384. list all flights on sunday from DALLAS to SAN FRANCISCO nonstop
P: list all flights on saturday from DALLAS to SAN FRANCISCO nonstop

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t1.stops = 0 ) AND t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS";

386. also show me the first flight from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON on a THURSDAY

P: first flights from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON on a THURSDAY
P: what is the earliest flight that goes from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON on THURSDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t6.day_name = "THURSDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t6.day_name = "THURSDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" );

389. shortest flight from ONTARIO CALIFORNIA to ORLANDO FLORIDA

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code WHERE ( t5.city_name = "ONTARIO" AND t4.city_name = "ORLANDO" AND t1.state_name = "CALIFORNIA" AND t2.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t3.time_elapsed = ( SELECT MIN ( t2.time_elapsed ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t5 ON t5.state_code = t3.state_code WHERE t4.city_name = "ONTARIO" AND t3.city_name = "ORLANDO" AND t1.state_name = "CALIFORNIA" AND t5.state_name = "FLORIDA" );

390. is there a meal on DL flight 852 from SAN FRANCISCO to DALLAS FORT WORTH

391. what is the aircraft type with the greatest seating capacity
P: what aircraft has the largest seating capacity

SELECT DISTINCT aircraft_code FROM aircraft WHERE capacity = ( SELECT MAX ( capacity ) FROM aircraft );

392. what is the lowest fare DL charges between DALLAS and DENVER
P: what is the lowest cost fare that DL has between DALLAS and DENVER
P: what is the cheapest fare from DALLAS to DENVER on DL

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t4 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t5.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t4.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t2.airline_code = "DL" ) AND t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id AND t3.airline_code = "DL" AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.departure_time < 1000 ) AND t4.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t2.airline_code = "UA";

P: find a nonstop flight between PITTSBURGH and PHILADELPHIA leaving in the afternoon and arriving near 5pm
P: i would like a nonstop flight between PITTSBURGH and PHILADELPHIA leaving in the afternoon and arriving in the vicinity of 5pm

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t5.arrival_time <= 1730 AND t5.arrival_time >= 1630 ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) AND t5.stops = 0;

PETERSBURG" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.airline_code = "TW" ) ) AND t2.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" ) AND t3.city_name = "ST. SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" AND t3.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY" ) AND t2.flight_number = 1222 ) AND t2.airline_code = "DL";

406. before 1000 o'clock on tuesday is there a 747 that flies from BALTIMORE to SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM equipment_sequence AS t1 JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.basic_type = "747" AND t2.departure_time < 1000 ) AND t6.day_number = 22 AND t6.month_number = 3 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE";

407. show me all flights arriving at SALT LAKE CITY
P: okay show me all the flights to SALT LAKE CITY
P: flights to SALT LAKE CITY
P: i would like to fly to SALT LAKE CITY
P: what are all the flights into SALT LAKE CITY 's airport
P: looking for a flight to SALT LAKE CITY

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE t2.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY";

408. when can i fly from PHILADELPHIA to DALLAS on a SATURDAY morning

SELECT DISTINCT t1.departure_time FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t6.day_name = "SATURDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200;

409. what time zone is DENVER in

SELECT DISTINCT time_zone_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "DENVER";

410. i'd like to arrange for two friends to fly into LOS ANGELES next saturday evening one of the people is coming from KANSAS CITY and the other is coming from LAS VEGAS

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t1.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t5.day_number = 26 AND t5.month_number = 7 AND t5.year = 1991 ) OR ( t5.day_number = 26 AND t5.month_number = 7 AND t5.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND ( t1.arrival_time <= 2200 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1800 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "LOS ANGELES" ) AND ( ( t4.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" ) );

411. show me all all flights from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA on wednesday which leave before 1200 and serve BREAKFAST

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM food_service AS t7 JOIN flight AS t1 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t1.departure_time < 1200 AND t7.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

412. i wish to book a flight from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA COACH discount fare

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t5.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t5.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t7 ON t7.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.class_type = "COACH" AND t2.discounted = "YES" ) AND t7.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

413. show me all flights out of BOSTON on 6 20 that have BUSINESS class

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t8.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t4.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t6.day_number = 20 AND t6.month_number = 6 AND t6.year = 1991 AND t2.class_type = "BUSINESS" ) AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON";

414. tell me about US flight 201
P: US 201

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE airline_code = "US" AND flight_number = 201;

415. how many stops on CO 1765 from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t5.stops FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t5.flight_number = 1765 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.airline_code = "CO";

416. what time are flights from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO on CO
P: what times does CO depart from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO
P: what time does CO depart from DENVER to go to SAN FRANCISCO
P: on CO give me the flight times from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO
P: when are the CO flights from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO
P: what time does the flight leave DENVER going to SAN FRANCISCO on CO

SELECT DISTINCT t5.departure_time FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t5.airline_code = "CO";

417. what airlines have flights from BOSTON to PHILADELPHIA that leave before 630
P: are there any airlines that have flights from BOSTON to PHILADELPHIA that leave before 630

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t1.departure_time < 630 ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

418. what flights are available from DENVER to DALLAS FORT WORTH in the afternoons
P: what afternoon flights are available between DENVER and DALLAS FORT WORTH

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t4.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

419. list flights from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO that serve only B

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM food_service AS t6 JOIN flight AS t1 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t1.meal_code = "B" OR t1.meal_code = "BB" ) AND t6.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

420. list nonstop flights from SFO to OAK that depart in the afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight AS t3 JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t2 ON t3.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.airport_code = "SFO" AND t2.airport_code = "OAK" ) AND t4.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t5.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) AND t3.stops = 0;

421. could you please list all of the classes of flights there are
P: what are the different classes that an airline offers

SELECT DISTINCT booking_class FROM class_of_service;

422. how many booking classes are there
P: how many different flight classes are there

SELECT DISTINCT COUNT ( DISTINCT booking_class ) FROM class_of_service;

423. how many of DL 's night flights are FIRST class

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t4.flight_id ) FROM fare AS t2 JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t2.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id WHERE ( t3.class_type = "FIRST" AND t4.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759 ) AND t4.airline_code = "DL";

424. i need a round trip flight from LOS ANGELES to TACOMA WASHINGTON
P: i'd like a round trip ticket from LOS ANGELES to TACOMA WASHINGTON

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t5.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t3 ON t1.fare_id = t3.fare_id WHERE ( t5.city_name = "TACOMA" AND t3.round_trip_cost is NOT null AND t2.state_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t6.city_name = "LOS ANGELES";

425. what do you have on monday from SFO to DENVER california
P: SFO to DENVER on monday november eleventh 1991

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t2.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t6.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( t3.city_name = "DENVER" AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.airport_code = "SFO";

426. list the cheapest one way flight from MIAMI FLORIDA to CHARLOTTE NORTH CAROLINA

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t7 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t7.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t5.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN state AS t3 ON t3.state_code = t7.state_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN state AS t4 ON t4.state_code = t6.state_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t7.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t6.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" AND t3.state_name = "FLORIDA" AND t4.state_name = "NORTH CAROLINA" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t6.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t5.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t3.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN state AS t7 ON t7.state_code = t4.state_code WHERE t5.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t4.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" AND t6.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t2.state_name = "FLORIDA" AND t7.state_name = "NORTH CAROLINA" ) AND t2.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t5.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

427. what is the earliest flight that i can take from BOSTON to BALTIMORE

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) OR ( t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM flight AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" );

428. i need information on flights from KANSAS CITY MISSOURI to SALT LAKE CITY UTAH i am interested in only those flights on DL

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code WHERE ( t5.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" AND t4.city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY" AND t1.state_name = "MISSOURI" AND t2.state_name = "UTAH" ) AND t3.airline_code = "DL";

429. what are the different classes of service and the prices for US

SELECT DISTINCT t5.booking_class , t2.fare_id FROM fare_basis AS t3 JOIN class_of_service AS t5 ON t3.booking_class = t5.booking_class JOIN fare AS t2 ON t2.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id WHERE t4.airline_code = "US";

430. is there an airline that services BOSTON WASHINGTON and DALLAS

SELECT DISTINCT t10.airline_code FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t5.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airline AS t10 ON t3.airline_code = t10.airline_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.airline_code = t10.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t1.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.airline_code = t10.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t4.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t6.city_name = "BOSTON" ) OR ( ( t5.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t4.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t6.city_name = "BOSTON" );

431. in flight meal OAKLAND to PHILADELPHIA saturday

433. i want a flight from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO that at least has 3 stop
P: list all flights from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO with at least 3 stops

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN flight_stop AS t6 ON t1.flight_id = t6.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t1.stops >= 3 ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON";

434. how far is OAK airport from downtown

SELECT DISTINCT t1.miles_distant FROM airport AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t4.airport_code = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE t1.airport_code = "OAK" AND t4.airport_code = "OAK";

435. find travel arrangements for a round trip flight from DALLAS to PITTSBURGH arriving after 2000 before 2200

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.round_trip_cost is NOT null AND t3.arrival_time < 2200 ) AND t3.arrival_time > 2000 ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS";

436. i need to know if there are any direct flights from ST. PETERSBURG FLORIDA to TACOMA WASHINGTON leaving preferably tomorrow morning

PETERSBURG" AND t1.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t3.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t3.connections = 0;

437. what kind of airplanes are used by DL flying between WASHINGTON and DENVER

438. very well i'm working on scenario three i'm interested in a flight on a 727 from WASHINGTON to ATLANTA GA

439. what airlines have nonstop early afternoon flights from BOSTON to OAKLAND
P: list the airlines that have nonstop afternoon flights from BOSTON to OAKLAND

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) AND t1.stops = 0;

440. show me all flights on thursday from ATLANTA to OAKLAND which arrive in OAKLAND before 1700 and serve a meal

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN food_service AS t7 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1700 ) AND t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA";

441. show me all the flights on DL and TW that go to ATLANTA in the morning

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.airline_code = "DL" ) OR ( t3.airline_code = "TW" ) ) AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200;

442. show me the flights that leave on THURSDAY mornings from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON and include whether meals are offered and what the prices are

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id , t4.flight_id , t4.meal_code FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN days AS t10 ON t4.flight_days = t10.days_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.basis_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( t6.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t10.day_name = "THURSDAY" ) AND t9.day_name = "THURSDAY" AND t4.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200;

444. on tuesday what flights leave CINCINNATI to SAN JOSE CALIFORNIA and leave after 1800
P: hi i need to go from CINCINNATI to SAN JOSE CALIFORNIA after 1800 on saturday

445. the cheapest flights between BOSTON and PHILADELPHIA which arrive between 3 and 1700 o'clock on tuesday

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t3.arrival_time < t3.departure_time ) AND t6.day_number = 22 AND t6.month_number = 3 AND t6.year = 1991 ) OR ( t6.day_number = 22 AND t6.month_number = 3 AND t6.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t3.arrival_time < t3.departure_time ) ) ) AND ( t3.arrival_time <= 1700 AND t3.arrival_time >= 1500 ) ) AND t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t2.arrival_time < t2.departure_time ) AND t6.day_number = 22 AND t6.month_number = 3 AND t6.year = 1991 ) OR ( t6.day_number = 22 AND t6.month_number = 3 AND t6.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t2.arrival_time < t2.departure_time ) ) ) AND ( t2.arrival_time <= 1700 AND t2.arrival_time >= 1500 ) ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

446. i want a flight that leaves from CHARLOTTE to NEWARK that leaves in the afternoon or evening
P: what flights depart from CHARLOTTE to NEWARK that leave in the afternoon or leave in the evening

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) OR ( t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) ) AND t3.city_name = "NEWARK" ) AND t4.city_name = "CHARLOTTE";

460. show me the latest nonstop flight from DENVER to WASHINGTON

PETERSBURG" AND t2.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" ) ) AND t4.day_number = 25 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991;

465. what 's the cheapest flight from CLEVELAND to MIAMI on AA
P: what is the cheapest flight on AA from CLEVELAND to MIAMI

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t5.city_name = "CLEVELAND" AND t4.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t3.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "CLEVELAND" AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t2.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

468. all round trip flights between NEW YORK and MIAMI FIRST class fare
P: all round trip flights between NEW YORK and MIAMI that are FIRST class
P: all round trip flights between NEW YORK and MIAMI FIRST fare
P: round trip flights from NEW YORK to MIAMI FIRST economy fare
P: information on round trip flights from NEW YORK to MIAMI FIRST class
P: information on FIRST class round trip from NEW YORK to MIAMI
P: show me FIRST class flights from NEW YORK to MIAMI round trip

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM fare AS t5 JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t5.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t6.city_name = "NEW YORK";

469. okay i'd like a nonstop flight from HOUSTON to MEMPHIS that arrives in MEMPHIS in the early afternoon on tuesday june first

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 3 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 3 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND ( t1.arrival_time <= 1400 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1200 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "MEMPHIS" ) AND t3.city_name = "HOUSTON" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

470. what is the cheapest round trip fare on CO 1291 round trip DENVER SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code , fare AS t4 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t5.city_name = "DENVER" AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.flight_number = 1291 ) AND t4.round_trip_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.round_trip_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t2.flight_number = 1291 ) AND t2.airline_code = "CO" ) AND t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id AND t3.airline_code = "CO" AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

471. show me flights from MILWAUKEE to ORLANDO on a THURSDAY before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t6.day_name = "THURSDAY" AND t1.departure_time < 1200 ) AND t2.city_name = "ORLANDO" ) AND t3.city_name = "MILWAUKEE";

472. show me all flights from NEW YORK to MIAMI leaving on a TUESDAY and show me all flights from MIAMI to NEW YORK leaving on SUNDAY
P: show me all flights from NEW YORK to MIAMI leaving on a TUESDAY and returning on SUNDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t6.day_name = "TUESDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) OR ( ( t2.city_name = "NEW YORK" AND t6.day_name = "SUNDAY" ) AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" );

473. how long does it take to get from ATL airport into the city of ATLANTA

SELECT DISTINCT t1.minutes_distant FROM airport AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE t3.airport_code = "ATL" AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA";

474. show me the most expensive fare

SELECT DISTINCT fare_id FROM fare WHERE one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t2.one_direction_cost ) FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id );

475. what is the schedule for flights between PITTSBURGH and BOSTON on the evening of 7 9

SELECT DISTINCT t1.arrival_time , t1.departure_time FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_leg AS t6 ON t2.flight_id = t6.flight_id JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t6.leg_flight JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t5.day_number = 9 AND t5.month_number = 7 AND t5.year = 1991 ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200;

476. flight from ONTARIO to ORLANDO that departs 9 hours before arriving

P: flights from LGA or JFK to CLEVELAND

478. AS flights to BURBANK please
P: how about arrivals for AS in BURBANK
P: what flights arrive in BURBANK from on AS
P: please list all AS flights into BURBANK
P: does AS fly into BURBANK
P: list the AS flights arriving in BURBANK

481. could you please tell me the first flight leaving BALTIMORE to SAN FRANCISCO on a 747 on 8 27

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.basic_type = "747" AND t6.day_number = 27 AND t6.month_number = 8 AND t6.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t2.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t2.departure_time ) FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t6 ON t1.aircraft_code = t6.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( t6.basic_type = "747" AND t5.day_number = 27 AND t5.month_number = 8 AND t5.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" );

482. list all DAILY flights between BOSTON and OAKLAND and between OAKLAND and BOSTON using DL

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) OR ( t4.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) ) AND t5.airline_code = "DL" ) AND t5.flight_days = "DAILY";

485. show me the flights from DENVER to SALT LAKE CITY next wednesday night after departure_time2 o'clock
P: i need flight information for a flight departing from DENVER to SALT LAKE CITY wednesday after 1700
P: i need flight information for flights departing from DENVER going back to SALT LAKE CITY wednesday after 1700
P: i need flight information for flights departing from DENVER to SALT LAKE CITY on wednesday after 1700
P: i need a flight from DENVER to SALT LAKE CITY departing wednesday after 1700
P: i need a flight from DENVER to SALT LAKE CITY on wednesday departing after 1700
P: give me the flights from DENVER to SALT LAKE CITY leaving after 1700 on wednesday
P: i need flight and airline information for a flight from DENVER to SALT LAKE CITY on monday departing after 1700

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE ( ( ( departure_time > 1700 AND flight_days IN ( SELECT days_code FROM days WHERE day_name IN ( SELECT day_name FROM date_day WHERE day_number = 21 AND month_number = 2 AND year = 1991 ) ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "SALT LAKE CITY" ) ) ) AND from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "DENVER" ) ) );

486. what is the latest flight from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA that serves a meal
P: the latest flight from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA please and i'd like a meal with that
P: find the latest flight from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA that serves a meal

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" );

487. what is the first flight from ATLANTA to BOSTON on thursday september fifth that leaves after 800

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time > 800 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 24 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time > 800 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" );

493. show me the shortest flight from BOSTON to DENVER which arrives in DENVER wednesday before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1200 ) AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t1.time_elapsed = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.time_elapsed ) FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1200 ) AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" );

494. i'd like to get a flight from WASHINGTON to OAKLAND with a stopover in DFW for 9 15

496. what flights are available from DENVER to BALTIMORE FIRST class on UA arriving 5 7 before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t7.flight_id FROM days AS t15 JOIN date_day AS t10 ON t15.day_name = t10.day_name JOIN flight AS t7 ON t7.flight_days = t15.days_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t7.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t8 ON t2.fare_id = t8.fare_id JOIN flight_fare AS t12 ON t7.flight_id = t12.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t14 ON t7.to_airport = t14.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t13 ON t7.from_airport = t13.airport_code JOIN fare_basis AS t5 ON t8.fare_basis_code = t5.fare_basis_code JOIN fare_basis AS t4 ON t8.fare_basis_code = t4.fare_basis_code JOIN days AS t16 ON t4.basis_days = t16.days_code JOIN fare AS t9 ON t12.fare_id = t9.fare_id JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t14.city_code JOIN date_day AS t11 ON t1.city_code = t13.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t3 ON t9.fare_basis_code = t3.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t13.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t7.arrival_time < 41 OR t7.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t7.departure_time > t7.arrival_time ) AND t10.day_number = 6 AND t10.month_number = 5 AND t10.year = 1991 ) AND t11.day_number = 6 AND t11.month_number = 5 AND t11.year = 1991 AND t5.class_type = "FIRST" ) OR ( ( t10.day_number = 7 AND t10.month_number = 5 AND t10.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t7.arrival_time < 41 OR t7.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t7.departure_time > t7.arrival_time ) ) AND t11.day_number = 7 AND t11.month_number = 5 AND t11.year = 1991 AND t5.class_type = "FIRST" ) ) AND t3.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t7.arrival_time < 1200 ) AND t6.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t1.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t7.airline_code = "UA";

497. i need a connecting flight on CO on 6 5 from CHICAGO to SEATTLE

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "SEATTLE" AND t4.day_number = 5 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t1.airline_code = "CO" ) AND t1.connections > 0;

499. is there a direct flight from ATLANTA to PHILADELPHIA that arrives in PHILADELPHIA around 12 noon

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.arrival_time <= 1230 AND t5.arrival_time >= 1130 ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.connections = 0;

500. and flight from OAKLAND to BOSTON leaving after 0

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.departure_time <= 600 AND t5.departure_time > 0 ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t4.city_name = "OAKLAND";

501. show me all flights to DALLAS that are less than 1500 dollars round trip

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t5.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t3 ON t2.fare_id = t3.fare_id WHERE t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t3.round_trip_cost < 1500;

502. what 's the difference between fare code Q and fare code F

SELECT DISTINCT booking_class , class_description , rank FROM class_of_service WHERE booking_class = "F" OR booking_class = "Q";

503. show me the flights from DENVER to BALTIMORE or WASHINGTON that arrive before or around noon

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) OR ( t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t2.state_code = "DC" ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1230 ) AND t4.city_name = "DENVER";

504. which airlines have DAILY flights from BOSTON to DALLAS

SELECT DISTINCT t6.airline_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airline AS t6 ON t1.airline_code = t6.airline_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.flight_days = "DAILY";

505. show me the earliest nonstop flight from WASHINGTON to SAN FRANCISCO
P: what is the earliest nonstop flight from WASHINGTON to SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.stops = 0 ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t4.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.stops = 0 ) AND t1.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" );

506. show me the flights from IAD to SAN FRANCISCO leaving after 1800

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t3 ON t4.from_airport = t3.airport_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t4.departure_time > 1800 ) AND t3.airport_code = "IAD";

507. i would like to fly from SEATTLE to CHICAGO next SUNDAY
P: i need a flight from SEATTLE to CHICAGO SUNDAY 8 six
P: show SUNDAY flights from SEATTLE to CHICAGO

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 27 AND t4.month_number = 8 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t7.day_name = "SUNDAY" ) AND t2.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t3.city_name = "SEATTLE";

508. how many flights does AA have from BOSTON to ATLANTA

509. what is the cost of a round trip ticket FIRST class between OAK and ATL

SELECT DISTINCT t6.fare_id FROM fare AS t6 JOIN fare_basis AS t4 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t4.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t3 ON t3.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.flight_id = t3.flight_id JOIN airport AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code WHERE ( t1.airport_code = "OAK" AND t2.airport_code = "ATL" AND t4.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t6.round_trip_cost is NOT null;

510. show me the airlines that use MKE
P: list all the airlines that fly into MKE

SELECT DISTINCT t3.airline_code FROM flight AS t2 JOIN airline AS t3 ON t2.airline_code = t3.airline_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.to_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE t1.airport_code = "MKE";

511. show me all overnight flights from WASHINGTON to SAN FRANCISCO and list their fares

512. what are the nonstop flights on HP or WN air from KANSAS CITY to BURBANK on saturday may 22

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.airline_code = "HP" ) OR ( t1.airline_code = "WN" ) ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "BURBANK" ) AND t3.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

513. what flights are there on wednesday evening or thursday morning from DENVER to SFO

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM days AS t6 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t6.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t2.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) ) AND t1.airport_code = "SFO" ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER";

514. please show all flights from PHILADELPHIA to DEN airport next sunday

515. what are the air restrictions on flights from PITTSBURGH to ATLANTA for the airfare of 416 dollars

SELECT DISTINCT t8.restriction_code FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN restriction AS t8 ON t8.restriction_code = t2.restriction_code WHERE t5.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t2.one_direction_cost = 416;

516. show me the most expensive one way FIRST class fare from BALTIMORE to DALLAS

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t6.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t5.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t6.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t5.city_name = "BALTIMORE" AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t6.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO";

517. i am interested in booking an early morning flight from DALLAS into HOUSTON on 2 22 and returning late in the evening of 2 22

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 2200 AND t1.departure_time >= 2000 ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t3.city_name = "HOUSTON" ) OR ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 800 ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "HOUSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" );

518. what type of aircraft leaves from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA at 800
P: on the 800 flight from SAN FRANCISCO to ATLANTA what type of aircraft is used

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t2.departure_time = 800 ) AND t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO";

519. how much does DL 746 cost

SELECT DISTINCT t2.fare_id FROM flight_fare AS t1 JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id WHERE t3.airline_code = "DL" AND t3.flight_number = 746;

520. i would like a flight from PITTSBURGH to BOSTON on friday morning after 800 o'clock
P: are there any later flights than 800 leaving from PITTSBURGH for BOSTON tomorrow evening
P: please show me flights from PITTSBURGH to BOSTON on saturday morning after 800

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.departure_time > 800 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200;

521. i want to travel from PITTSBURGH to OAKLAND around midnight could you give me the flights
P: could you tell me the flights leaving PITTSBURGH around midnight for OAKLAND

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.departure_time >= 2330 OR t5.departure_time < 30 ) AND t3.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

522. AA flight 4400 from CINCINNATI to HOUSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight_leg AS t5 ON t1.flight_id = t5.flight_id JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_id = t5.leg_flight WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "HOUSTON" AND t2.airline_code = "AA" AND t2.flight_number = 4400 ) AND t4.city_name = "CINCINNATI" ) AND t1.airline_code = "AA";

523. i need a plane that arrives in NEW YORK by 1800 o'clock pm on friday and leaves from CINCINNATI
P: what flights depart CINCINNATI and arrive by 1800 friday in NEW YORK
P: please find all the flights from CINCINNATI to any airport in the NEW YORK area that arrive next saturday before 1800

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time <= 1800 ) AND t2.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) AND t3.city_name = "CINCINNATI";

525. show me the cheapest one way flights from PITTSBURGH to DALLAS leaving PITTSBURGH between 1200 and 1400

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( ( t3.departure_time <= 1400 AND t3.departure_time >= 1200 ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t5.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( ( t2.departure_time <= 1400 AND t2.departure_time >= 1200 ) AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t4.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

526. what flights leave SAN FRANCISCO after 2000 and go to DALLAS FORT WORTH

528. how many DAILY US flights are there between PHILADELPHIA and PITTSBURGH

529. what are the latest flights from BOSTON to DALLAS on the evening of 7 7

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t4.day_number = 7 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t4.day_number = 7 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 );

530. what type of aircraft leaves from BOSTON to WASHINGTON at 900 during a weekday

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM flight AS t2 JOIN days AS t9 ON t2.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t2.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN days AS t10 ON t2.flight_days = t10.days_code JOIN days AS t11 ON t2.flight_days = t11.days_code JOIN days AS t12 ON t2.flight_days = t12.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t9.day_name = "THURSDAY" AND t8.day_name = "FRIDAY" ) AND t10.day_name = "WEDNESDAY" ) AND t11.day_name = "TUESDAY" ) AND t12.day_name = "MONDAY" ) AND t2.departure_time = 900 ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

P: show me the QX fare flights between BOSTON and SAN FRANCISCO on UA
P: list all UA flights from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO with fare code QX

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.fare_basis_code = "QX" ) AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.airline_code = "UA";

532. on EA flight 825 from ATLANTA to DENVER can you tell me what type of aircraft used before 1200

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE ( ( ( t2.departure_time < 1200 AND t2.flight_number = 825 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t2.airline_code = "EA";

541. what is the earliest flight going from SAN FRANCISCO to DALLAS on monday august nineteenth

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 );

542. i'd like to find a flight from MIAMI FLORIDA to LAS VEGAS NEVADA that would arrive before 1600 on sunday

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t6 ON t9.day_name = t6.day_name JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t3.arrival_time < 41 OR t3.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t3.departure_time > t3.arrival_time ) AND t6.day_number = 27 AND t6.month_number = 8 AND t6.year = 1991 ) OR ( t6.day_number = 27 AND t6.month_number = 8 AND t6.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t3.arrival_time < 41 OR t3.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t3.departure_time > t3.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t3.arrival_time < 1600 ) AND t4.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" AND t2.state_name = "NEVADA" ) AND t5.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t1.state_name = "FLORIDA";

543. what 's the earliest flight from BOSTON to BWI that serves LUNCH
P: what is the earliest flight from BOSTON to BWI that serves a LUNCH

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM flight AS t5 JOIN airport AS t3 ON t5.to_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t4 ON t4.meal_code = t5.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.airport_code = "BWI" AND t4.meal_description = "LUNCH" ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM flight AS t5 JOIN airport AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t3 ON t3.meal_code = t5.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( t4.airport_code = "BWI" AND t3.meal_description = "LUNCH" ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" );

550. what is the cheapest flight from BOSTON to BWI

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code , fare AS t4 , flight_fare AS t2 WHERE ( t1.airport_code = "BWI" AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t4.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t3.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t2.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE t1.airport_code = "BWI" AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t2.fare_id = t4.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t2.flight_id;

551. please list the flights from ST. PAUL to KANSAS CITY on FRIDAY night that serve meals

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN food_service AS t6 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 2400 AND t1.departure_time >= 1800 ) AND t7.day_name = "FRIDAY" ) OR ( ( t1.departure_time <= 600 AND t1.departure_time >= 0 ) AND t7.day_name = "SATURDAY" ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) AND t3.city_name = "ST. PAUL";
