553. last nonstop flight from LOS ANGELES to PITTSBURGH on monday night

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759 ) AND t1.departure_time <= 600 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( ( ( t1.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759 ) AND t1.departure_time > 1759 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t3.city_name = "LOS ANGELES" ) AND t1.stops = 0 ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759 ) AND t1.departure_time <= 600 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( ( ( t1.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759 ) AND t1.departure_time > 1759 ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t3.city_name = "LOS ANGELES" ) AND t1.stops = 0 );

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time <= 1245 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1115 ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

564. what is the cost of the AIR TAXI OPERATION at PHL airport

SELECT DISTINCT t2.ground_fare FROM ground_service AS t2 JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.airport_code = t1.airport_code WHERE t1.airport_code = "PHL" AND t2.transport_type = "AIR TAXI OPERATION";

565. i would like to book a flight for 5 26 going from TAMPA to MILWAUKEE a direct flight if possible

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "MILWAUKEE" AND t4.day_number = 26 AND t4.month_number = 5 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "TAMPA" ) AND t1.connections = 0;

566. i want to fly from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO with at least one stop
P: list all flights from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO with more than 3 stops

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t5.stops > 3 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

567. what kind of plane flies from BOSTON to ATLANTA after 1700
P: what type of aircraft leaving after 1700 from BOSTON to ATLANTA
P: i'm traveling from BOSTON to ATLANTA and i'd like to go sometime after 1700 but i want to know what kind of airplane it 's on

SELECT DISTINCT t5.aircraft_code FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t2.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t5 ON t1.aircraft_code = t5.aircraft_code WHERE t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t2.departure_time > 1700;

568. what are the fares for flights between ATLANTA and DFW provided by DL

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t3.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t4 ON t2.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE ( t1.airport_code = "DFW" AND t5.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t3.airline_code = "DL";

569. between BOSTON and DENVER i'd like a flight that takes the least amount of stops to get to BOSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.stops = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.stops ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE t2.city_name = "DENVER" AND t1.city_name = "BOSTON" );

570. show me all the night fares between PHILADELPHIA and SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t5.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.departure_time NOT BETWEEN 601 AND 1759;

571. show me all flights that go from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO on tuesday and go from CHICAGO to KANSAS CITY on sunday
P: i need to fly from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO leaving next wednesday and returning the following day
P: what flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO leave next wednesday returning the following day

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "CHICAGO" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" ) OR ( ( t2.city_name = "KANSAS CITY" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "CHICAGO" );

572. how many flights come from DENVER to BALTIMORE on 7 19

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t1.flight_id ) FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) AND t4.day_number = 18 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 19 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( t1.arrival_time < t1.departure_time ) ) ) AND ( t3.city_name = "DENVER" AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" );

573. which airlines fly from BWI to DALLAS FORT WORTH

SELECT DISTINCT t7.airline_code FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airline AS t7 ON t2.airline_code = t7.airline_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t3.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t1.airport_code = "BWI";

574. i'd like an afternoon flight from ATLANTA to SAN FRANCISCO with a stopover in DENVER arriving i'd say about mealtime

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t8 ON t8.stop_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t8.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time <= 2000 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1700 ) AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

575. please list the shortest 1 stop flight from ONTARIO CALIFORNIA to ORLANDO FLORIDA

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t5.state_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "ORLANDO" AND t3.stops = 1 AND t2.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t5.city_name = "ONTARIO" AND t1.state_name = "CALIFORNIA" ) AND t3.time_elapsed = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.time_elapsed ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN state AS t3 ON t3.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t5.state_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "ORLANDO" AND t1.stops = 1 AND t3.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t5.city_name = "ONTARIO" AND t2.state_name = "CALIFORNIA" );

576. find me the latest return flight from ATLANTA to BOSTON on the same day

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND NOT ( t5.arrival_time < t5.departure_time ) ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code WHERE ( t1.city_name = "BOSTON" AND NOT ( t5.arrival_time < t5.departure_time ) ) AND t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" );

577. i would like a flight from WASHINGTON to BOSTON flight 324 on 8 20

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 8 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.flight_number = 324 ) AND t2.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON";

578. list nonstop flights from BALTIMORE WASHINGTON to OAKLAND that arrive between 1645 and 1715

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t1.arrival_time <= 1715 AND t1.arrival_time >= 1645 ) AND t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND ( ( t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) ) ) AND t1.stops = 0;

579. hi i want a round trip ticket to DALLAS

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t2 ON t5.flight_id = t2.flight_id JOIN fare AS t3 ON t2.fare_id = t3.fare_id WHERE t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t3.round_trip_cost is NOT null;

580. what city is MCO
P: what city is the airport MCO in

SELECT DISTINCT t2.city_code FROM airport AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE t3.airport_code = "MCO";

581. what is the last flight from SAN FRANCISCO to WASHINGTON in the evening
P: what is the latest evening flight leaving SAN FRANCISCO for WASHINGTON

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t1.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 );

582. is there a red eye flight from SAN JOSE to NASHVILLE on wednesday the nineteenth of may

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 2359 AND t1.departure_time >= 2100 ) OR ( t1.departure_time <= 300 AND t1.departure_time >= 0 ) ) AND ( t1.arrival_time <= 1200 AND t1.arrival_time >= 500 ) ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t2.city_name = "NASHVILLE" ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN JOSE";

583. show me the airlines from DAL

SELECT DISTINCT t3.airline_code FROM flight AS t2 JOIN airline AS t3 ON t2.airline_code = t3.airline_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.from_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE t1.airport_code = "DAL";

584. show flights from LAS VEGAS to NEW YORK on TW airlines with fare information
P: please list the TW flights from LAS VEGAS to NEW YORK and fare

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t5.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" AND t4.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) AND t3.airline_code = "TW";

585. what FIRST class airplane goes from PHILADELPHIA to SAN FRANCISCO and stops in DALLAS in the afternoon on monday

SELECT DISTINCT t13.aircraft_code FROM days AS t21 JOIN date_day AS t14 ON t21.day_name = t14.day_name JOIN flight AS t7 ON t7.flight_days = t21.days_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t7.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN flight_stop AS t20 ON t7.flight_id = t20.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t17 ON t7.to_airport = t17.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t5 ON t7.aircraft_code_sequence = t5.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN flight_leg AS t3 ON t7.flight_id = t3.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t16 ON t7.from_airport = t16.airport_code JOIN flight AS t8 ON t8.flight_id = t3.leg_flight JOIN airport_service AS t19 ON t8.from_airport = t19.airport_code JOIN fare AS t11 ON t7.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t18 ON t20.stop_airport = t18.airport_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t17.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t8.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t12 ON t12.city_code = t16.city_code JOIN city AS t9 ON t9.city_code = t19.city_code JOIN aircraft AS t13 ON t5.aircraft_code = t13.aircraft_code JOIN city AS t15 ON t7.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t10 ON t10.city_code = t18.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t4 ON t11.fare_basis_code = t4.fare_basis_code WHERE ( ( ( t14.day_number = 21 AND t14.month_number = 2 AND t14.year = 1991 AND t4.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t10.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t6.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND ( ( t8.arrival_time <= 1800 AND t8.arrival_time >= 1200 ) AND t15.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t12.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t9.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA";

586. i'd like to arrange a trip to BALTIMORE on 1 1

587. list the flights that leave from PHILADELPHIA to ATLANTA early thursday morning before 800

588. on 5 4 ATLANTA to DENVER DL flight 257

589. return from MIAMI to NEW YORK on FF on SATURDAY

590. do i get a meal on the ATLANTA to BWI flight EA 210

P: please list all flights on UA and NW which go to DENVER

592. show flights FIRST class on AA from PHILADELPHIA to DALLAS FORT WORTH

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t6.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t10 ON t4.to_airport = t10.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN fare AS t3 ON t1.fare_id = t3.fare_id JOIN city AS t7 ON t7.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t3.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t10.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t6.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t5.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t7.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.airline_code = "AA";

593. show me the flights on DL from ATLANTA in the morning

594. please tell me which airline has the most departures from ATLANTA

SELECT DISTINCT COUNT ( * ) , t3.airline_code FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" GROUP BY t3.airline_code;

595. what is the flight schedule of the F28 from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE

SELECT DISTINCT t2.arrival_time , t2.departure_time FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight_leg AS t7 ON t3.flight_id = t7.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN equipment_sequence AS t1 ON t3.aircraft_code_sequence = t1.aircraft_code_sequence JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_id = t7.leg_flight JOIN aircraft AS t6 ON t1.aircraft_code = t6.aircraft_code WHERE ( t6.aircraft_code = "F28" AND t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t5.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

596. list nonstop flights from LOS ANGELES to PITTSBURGH which arrive on monday after 1700

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time > 1700 ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t3.city_name = "LOS ANGELES" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

597. show me one way flights from INDIANAPOLIS to MEMPHIS departing before 1000 FIRST class
P: one way flights from INDIANAPOLIS to MEMPHIS leaving before 1000 on any day and FIRST class
P: please show me FIRST class flights from INDIANAPOLIS to MEMPHIS one way leaving before 1000

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM fare AS t5 JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" AND t4.departure_time < 1000 ) AND t3.city_name = "MEMPHIS" ) AND t6.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS";

598. may i please see airlines and flight numbers from NEW YORK to TORONTO on the same date 6 17 also arriving in TORONTO before 1200 thank you

SELECT DISTINCT t7.airline_code , t1.flight_number FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airline AS t7 ON t1.airline_code = t7.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 17 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t1.arrival_time < 1200 ) AND t2.city_name = "TORONTO" ) AND t3.city_name = "NEW YORK";

599. describe SAN FRANCISCO airport
P: please list information regarding SAN FRANCISCO airport

SELECT DISTINCT t3.airport_code , t3.airport_location , t3.airport_name , t3.country_name , t3.minimum_connect_time , t3.state_code , t3.time_zone_code FROM airport AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO";

600. show me the flights from PITTSBURGH to BALTIMORE arriving in BALTIMORE on 6 14

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 14 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 14 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND ( t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" );

601. show departures and arrivals in ATLANTA for american airlines
P: what are all of the flights into and out of ATLANTA 's airport

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM flight AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.from_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" );

602. round trip flights from MIAMI to NEW YORK nonstop flights if possible
P: show me round trips from MIAMI to NEW YORK nonstop
P: show me all round trip flights from MIAMI to NEW YORK nonstop

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t2 ON t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "NEW YORK" AND t2.round_trip_cost is NOT null ) AND t5.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t3.stops = 0;

603. how many flights go from SAN FRANCISCO to PHILADELPHIA on 8 18
P: how many flights are there between SAN FRANCISCO and PHILADELPHIA on 8 18

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t1.flight_id ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t4.day_number = 18 AND t4.month_number = 8 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO";

604. what flights are there on wednesday evening from DENVER to SFO

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM days AS t6 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t6.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t1.airport_code = "SFO" AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200;

605. all flights from CHARLOTTE to anywhere on US around 1pm

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.departure_time <= 1330 AND t5.departure_time >= 1230 ) ) AND t4.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" ) AND t5.airline_code = "US";

606. are there any early flights from ATLANTA to WASHINGTON on THURSDAY mornings

610. please show me UA nonstop flights between BOSTON and SAN FRANCISCO departing around 5 in the evening

611. show me all connecting flights on UA between BOSTON and SAN FRANCISCO
P: which UA flights from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO make connections

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t5.airline_code = "UA" ) AND t5.connections > 0;

612. does flight DL 323 / DL 229 from BOSTON to DENVER stop in PHILADELPHIA

SELECT DISTINCT t10.flight_id , t10.stop_number FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t3.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN flight_stop AS t10 ON t1.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t10.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t1.from_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t10.stop_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight_leg AS t6 ON t1.flight_id = t6.flight_id JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_id = t6.leg_flight WHERE ( ( t2.flight_number = 229 OR t2.flight_number = 323 ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER" AND t2.airline_code = "DL" ) AND t5.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON";

613. i need a flight from BOS to ATLANTA this afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN days AS t6 ON t2.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t6.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t4.day_number = 5 AND t4.month_number = 9 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t1.airport_code = "BOS" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

614. what is the last flight from SAN FRANCISCO to DALLAS FORT WORTH

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t3.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" );

615. which is the flight number for the US flight from PHILADELPHIA to BOSTON is it 279 or is it 137338

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.flight_number = 137338 OR t5.flight_number = 279 ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t5.airline_code = "US";

616. show me flights from MILWAUKEE to ORLANDO on wednesday evening or THURSDAY mornings

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t7.day_name = "THURSDAY" ) OR ( ( t1.departure_time BETWEEN 1800 AND 2200 ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) ) AND t2.city_name = "ORLANDO" ) AND t3.city_name = "MILWAUKEE";

617. from WASHINGTON to PHILADELPHIA departing in the afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN state AS t1 ON t1.state_code = t4.state_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" AND t1.state_code = "DC" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

620. how much is a LIMOUSINE between DALLAS/FORT WORTH INTERNATIONAL international airport and DALLAS

622. what is your earliest morning flight from INDIANAPOLIS to CHARLOTTE

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t3.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" ) AND t4.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t1.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" ) AND t2.city_name = "INDIANAPOLIS" );

623. the cheapest flights from ATLANTA to PHILADELPHIA that arrive after 12pm on a TUESDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight AS t3 JOIN days AS t8 ON t3.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t3.arrival_time < t3.departure_time ) AND t8.day_name = "MONDAY" ) OR ( t8.day_name = "TUESDAY" AND NOT ( t3.arrival_time < t3.departure_time ) ) ) AND t3.arrival_time > 1200 ) AND t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t5.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM flight AS t2 JOIN days AS t8 ON t2.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t2.arrival_time < t2.departure_time ) AND t8.day_name = "MONDAY" ) OR ( t8.day_name = "TUESDAY" AND NOT ( t2.arrival_time < t2.departure_time ) ) ) AND t2.arrival_time > 1200 ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

624. what flights from KANSAS CITY to CHICAGO arrive at CHICAGO at 1900 next wednesday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 23 AND t4.month_number = 4 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time = 1900 ) AND t2.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t3.city_name = "KANSAS CITY";

625. what is the cheapest flight flying from BOSTON to ATLANTA before 800

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.departure_time < 800 ) AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t2.departure_time < 800 ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

627. i'd like a list of the flights from OAKLAND to DALLAS FORT WORTH on sunday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t1.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN days AS t9 ON t1.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t2.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t5.day_number = 27 AND t5.month_number = 8 AND t5.year = 1991 ) AND t4.city_name = "OAKLAND";

628. show me all fares between PHILADELPHIA and SAN FRANCISCO that are less than 200 dollars one way

SELECT DISTINCT t3.fare_id FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN fare AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t3.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.one_direction_cost < 200 AND t3.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t5.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA";

629. what is the FIRST class fare on UA flight 352 from DENVER to BOSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t4.flight_number = 352 ) AND t6.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" AND t4.airline_code = "UA";

630. show me the cheapest flights round trip from NEW YORK to SAN JOSE arriving in SAN JOSE before 1900

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "SAN JOSE" AND t3.arrival_time < 1900 ) AND t5.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) AND t2.round_trip_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.round_trip_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( t3.city_name = "SAN JOSE" AND t2.arrival_time < 1900 ) AND t4.city_name = "NEW YORK" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

631. what is the first flight from BOSTON to STAPLETON airport for tomorrow

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM days AS t6 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t6.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t1.airport_name LIKE "STAPLETON" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t2.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t2.departure_time ) FROM days AS t6 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t6.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t2.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( t1.airport_name LIKE "STAPLETON" AND t4.day_number = 20 AND t4.month_number = 1 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" );

632. i would like to leave around 7 o'clock in the morning

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE departure_time <= 730 AND departure_time >= 630;

633. what are connecting flights from CHICAGO to SEATTLE on 6 5
P: what are connecting flights from CHICAGO into SEATTLE on 6 5

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "SEATTLE" AND t4.day_number = 5 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "CHICAGO" ) AND t1.connections > 0;

634. what is the code for BUSINESS class

SELECT DISTINCT t1.fare_basis_code FROM fare AS t1 JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t1.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE t2.class_type = "BUSINESS";

635. can you show me evening flights from NASHVILLE to HOUSTON that serve DINNER

636. how much is a US BOSTON to PITTSBURGH DAILY nonstop flight

639. list UA flights from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO on TUESDAY or WEDNESDAY

640. how many stops are on all flights from BOSTON to SAN FRANCISCO that depart before 1200

641. how many nonstop flights going from DALLAS to OAKLAND 7 27

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t1.flight_id ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" AND t4.day_number = 27 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

642. all flights from MONTREAL less than 150 dollars

643. i want to fly from OAKLAND at 1300 and arrive in PHILADELPHIA at 1700 in the morning
P: i want to leave OAKLAND at 1300 and arrive in PHILADELPHIA at 1700 in the morning
P: i would like a flight from OAKLAND to PHILADELPHIA at one in the afternoon arriving at 1700

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t5.arrival_time = 1700 AND t5.departure_time = 1300 ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.city_name = "OAKLAND";

644. what is the earliest flight from WASHINGTON to SAN FRANCISCO on friday that serves BREAKFAST

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t8 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN food_service AS t7 ON t7.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t4.day_number = 25 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t7.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN food_service AS t8 ON t8.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.day_number = 25 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 AND t8.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" );

645. please list the flight schedule from BALTIMORE to SAN FRANCISCO on FRIDAY nights

SELECT DISTINCT t1.arrival_time , t1.departure_time FROM flight AS t2 JOIN days AS t8 ON t2.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_leg AS t5 ON t2.flight_id = t5.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t5.leg_flight WHERE ( ( ( ( t2.departure_time <= 2400 AND t2.departure_time >= 1800 ) AND t8.day_name = "FRIDAY" ) OR ( ( t2.departure_time <= 600 AND t2.departure_time >= 0 ) AND t8.day_name = "SATURDAY" ) ) AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE";

646. okay what i would like to know is does TW flight 505 from CHARLOTTE to LAS VEGAS with a stop in ST. LOUIS serve DINNER that 's TW flight 505 or 163

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM flight AS t2 JOIN flight_leg AS t8 ON t2.flight_id = t8.flight_id JOIN flight_leg AS t7 ON t2.flight_id = t7.flight_id JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.flight_id = t8.leg_flight JOIN food_service AS t13 ON t1.flight_id = t7.leg_flight JOIN flight_stop AS t12 ON t2.flight_id = t12.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t10 ON t2.to_airport = t10.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t2.from_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_id = t7.leg_flight JOIN airport_service AS t11 ON t12.stop_airport = t11.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t10.city_code JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t9.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t11.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t3.flight_number = 505 AND t1.flight_number = 163 ) AND t13.meal_description = "DINNER" ) AND t4.city_name = "ST. LOUIS" ) AND t5.city_name = "LAS VEGAS" ) AND t6.city_name = "CHARLOTTE" ) AND t2.airline_code = "TW";

647. i would like the time of your earliest flight in the morning from PHILADELPHIA to WASHINGTON on AA

SELECT DISTINCT t5.departure_time FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( t5.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t5.airline_code = "AA" ) AND t1.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t2.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t5.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200 );

648. show me the flights arriving in BALTIMORE on 6 15 leaving either from DENVER or DALLAS

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t9 JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t1.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t5.day_number = 14 AND t5.month_number = 6 AND t5.year = 1991 ) OR ( t5.day_number = 15 AND t5.month_number = 6 AND t5.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND ( ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" ) OR ( t3.city_name = "DALLAS" ) );

649. i need a flight to ATLANTA this afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN days AS t5 ON t4.flight_days = t5.days_code JOIN date_day AS t3 ON t5.day_name = t3.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "ATLANTA" AND t3.day_number = 5 AND t3.month_number = 9 AND t3.year = 1991 ) AND t4.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

650. what is the departure time of the latest flight of UA from DENVER to BOSTON

SELECT DISTINCT t5.departure_time FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "DENVER" AND t3.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.airline_code = "UA" ) AND t5.departure_time = ( SELECT MAX ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t3 ON t2.city_code = t3.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t3.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t5.to_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t1 ON t1.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( t2.city_name = "DENVER" AND t1.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t5.airline_code = "UA" );

651. what 's the cheapest FIRST class airfare from PITTSBURGH to SAN FRANCISCO

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE ( t6.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" ) AND t5.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t6.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code WHERE t5.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t4.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" );

652. for each airline flying between BOSTON and SAN FRANCISCO what is the earliest flight

SELECT DISTINCT t5.airline_code , MIN ( t5.departure_time ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" GROUP BY t5.airline_code;

653. instead of denver can i have the same flight from TORONTO to SAN DIEGO but stopping in DTW
P: locate flights from TORONTO to SAN DIEGO stopping in DTW
P: get flight from TORONTO to SAN DIEGO stopping at DTW

SELECT DISTINCT t2.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t2.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN flight_stop AS t7 ON t2.flight_id = t7.flight_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN airport AS t1 ON t7.stop_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE ( t1.airport_code = "DTW" AND t3.city_name = "SAN DIEGO" ) AND t4.city_name = "TORONTO";

654. show me all the types of aircraft

655. all AS flights to everywhere if you can
P: list all AS flights

656. i need a listing of flights from NEW YORK to MONTREAL CANADA departing thursday in the morning

657. i would like to know the latest flight on wednesday you have leaving from OAKLAND to SALT LAKE CITY which offers a meal

659. please show me the cost of flight UA 201 from BOSTON to DENVER and flight UA 343 from BOSTON to DENVER

SELECT DISTINCT t4.fare_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t4 ON t1.fare_id = t4.fare_id WHERE ( ( ( t3.flight_number = 201 OR t3.flight_number = 343 ) AND t2.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t3.airline_code = "UA";

660. list all flights from TAMPA FLORIDA to MIAMI that are the cheapest one way

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t6.state_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t8.city_code , fare AS t3 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( t6.city_name = "TAMPA" AND t5.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t2.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t3.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t6.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN state AS t2 ON t2.state_code = t5.state_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id WHERE t5.city_name = "TAMPA" AND t4.city_name = "MIAMI" AND t6.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t2.state_name = "FLORIDA" ) AND t3.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t1.fare_id = t3.fare_id AND t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

661. what 's the most expensive way i can fly to WASHINGTON

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code , fare AS t3 , flight AS t5 , flight_fare AS t2 WHERE t4.city_name = "WASHINGTON" AND t3.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MAX ( t3.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t5 ON t4.flight_id = t5.flight_id JOIN fare AS t3 ON t5.fare_id = t3.fare_id WHERE t2.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t2.fare_id = t3.fare_id AND t5.flight_id = t2.flight_id AND t5.to_airport = t1.airport_code;

662. airlines that fly to SAN FRANCISCO from PITTSBURGH on friday
P: tell me which airlines have flights from PITTSBURGH to SAN FRANCISCO on monday september second

SELECT DISTINCT t7.airline_code FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airline AS t7 ON t1.airline_code = t7.airline_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t4.day_number = 21 AND t4.month_number = 2 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

663. how many AS flights are there to BURBANK
P: how many flights does AS have to BURBANK

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t3.flight_id ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code WHERE t2.city_name = "BURBANK" AND t3.airline_code = "AS";

664. what ground transportation is available from the PITTSBURGH airport to downtown and how much does it cost

SELECT DISTINCT t5.ground_fare , t5.transport_type FROM airport AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.airport_code = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN ground_service AS t5 ON t5.airport_code = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t5.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE t3.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH";

665. list all nonstop flights from LOS ANGELES to PITTSBURGH which arrive before 1700 on tuesday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM days AS t7 JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 3 AND t4.year = 1991 ) OR ( t4.day_number = 22 AND t4.month_number = 3 AND t4.year = 1991 AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time < 1700 ) AND t2.city_name = "PITTSBURGH" ) AND t3.city_name = "LOS ANGELES" ) AND t1.stops = 0;

668. what 's the price of the least expensive FIRST class round trip ticket on US from CLEVELAND to MIAMI

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t6 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t4.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t4.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t5.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( ( t6.city_name = "CLEVELAND" AND t3.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" AND t4.airline_code = "US" ) AND t5.round_trip_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t6.round_trip_cost ) FROM city AS t5 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t5.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN fare AS t6 ON t1.fare_id = t6.fare_id JOIN fare_basis AS t2 ON t6.fare_basis_code = t2.fare_basis_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t8.city_code WHERE ( t5.city_name = "CLEVELAND" AND t4.city_name = "MIAMI" ) AND t2.class_type = "FIRST" AND t3.airline_code = "US" );

669. i need an early flight from DENVER to SAN FRANCISCO please and i would like BREAKFAST served on that

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM food_service AS t6 JOIN flight AS t1 ON t6.meal_code = t1.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t1.departure_time <= 1000 AND t1.departure_time >= 0 ) AND t6.meal_description = "BREAKFAST" ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "DENVER";

670. what round trip tickets are there from CLEVELAND to MIAMI on US that arrive before 1600

672. i have two friends that would like to visit me on wednesday here in WASHINGTON one of them lives in DENVER and the other lives in MIAMI

678. what is the earliest flight that has no stops from WASHINGTON to SAN FRANCISCO on friday

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t4.day_number = 25 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t1.stops = 0 ) AND t1.departure_time = ( SELECT MIN ( t1.departure_time ) FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t1 ON t1.to_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.from_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN days AS t7 ON t1.flight_days = t7.days_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t7.day_name = t4.day_name WHERE ( ( t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t4.day_number = 25 AND t4.month_number = 6 AND t4.year = 1991 ) AND t3.city_name = "WASHINGTON" ) AND t1.stops = 0 );

PETERSBURG" ) AND t2.airline_code = "TW" ) AND t2.departure_time BETWEEN 0 AND 1200;

688. list lowest cost flight from DALLAS to BALTIMORE that serves a meal

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t8 ON t8.meal_code = t3.meal_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( t4.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t5.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN flight AS t2 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN food_service AS t8 ON t8.meal_code = t2.meal_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE" ) AND t4.city_name = "DALLAS" ) AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

689. give me the cheapest one way flights between BOSTON and PHILADELPHIA which arrive after 1200 on a TUESDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM flight AS t3 JOIN days AS t8 ON t3.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t3.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code , fare AS t2 , flight_fare AS t1 WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t3.arrival_time < t3.departure_time ) AND t8.day_name = "MONDAY" ) OR ( t8.day_name = "TUESDAY" AND NOT ( t3.arrival_time < t3.departure_time ) ) ) AND t3.arrival_time > 1200 ) AND t4.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t5.city_name = "BOSTON" ) AND t2.one_direction_cost = ( SELECT MIN ( t5.one_direction_cost ) FROM flight AS t2 JOIN days AS t8 ON t2.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t2.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t2.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id WHERE ( ( ( ( ( t2.arrival_time < t2.departure_time ) AND t8.day_name = "MONDAY" ) OR ( t8.day_name = "TUESDAY" AND NOT ( t2.arrival_time < t2.departure_time ) ) ) AND t2.arrival_time > 1200 ) AND t3.city_name = "PHILADELPHIA" ) AND t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t5.round_trip_required = "NO" ) AND t2.round_trip_required = "NO" AND t1.fare_id = t2.fare_id AND t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id;

690. list nonstop flights from BWI washington airport to OAKLAND that depart in the afternoon

SELECT DISTINCT t4.flight_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t2.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t4 ON t4.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport AS t3 ON t4.from_airport = t3.airport_code WHERE ( ( t3.airport_code = "BWI" AND t2.city_name = "OAKLAND" ) AND t4.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800 ) AND t4.stops = 0;

691. flights from MILWAUKEE to PHOENIX on saturday or sunday AA
P: give me the flights from MILWAUKEE to PHOENIX on saturday or sunday on AA

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t9 ON t1.flight_days = t9.days_code JOIN date_day AS t5 ON t9.day_name = t5.day_name JOIN days AS t8 ON t1.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN date_day AS t4 ON t8.day_name = t4.day_name JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t1.to_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.from_airport = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t6.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t1.airline_code = "AA" ) AND ( ( t5.year = 1991 AND t5.month_number = 7 AND t5.day_number = 26 ) OR ( t4.year = 1991 AND t4.month_number = 7 AND t4.day_number = 26 ) ) ) AND t2.city_name = "PHOENIX" ) AND t3.city_name = "MILWAUKEE";

692. my question is i want to go to SAN FRANCISCO and i live in DENVER and i would like to fly on UA do you have an early flight

SELECT DISTINCT t5.flight_id FROM city AS t3 JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code WHERE ( ( t3.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" AND t5.departure_time <= 1000 ) AND t4.city_name = "DENVER" ) AND t5.airline_code = "UA";

693. what is a flight that goes from BALTIMORE to SAN FRANCISCO and arrives at SAN FRANCISCO at 2000 on a FRIDAY

SELECT DISTINCT t1.flight_id FROM flight AS t1 JOIN days AS t6 ON t1.flight_days = t6.days_code JOIN airport_service AS t5 ON t1.to_airport = t5.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t4 ON t1.from_airport = t4.airport_code JOIN city AS t2 ON t2.city_code = t5.city_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t4.city_code WHERE ( ( ( ( ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) AND t6.day_name = "THURSDAY" ) OR ( t6.day_name = "FRIDAY" AND NOT ( ( t1.arrival_time < 41 OR t1.time_elapsed >= 60 ) AND t1.departure_time > t1.arrival_time ) ) ) AND t1.arrival_time = 2000 ) AND t2.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.city_name = "BALTIMORE";

694. what is the fare from SAN FRANCISCO to DALLAS FORT WORTH on DL flight 852

SELECT DISTINCT t5.fare_id FROM city AS t2 JOIN airport_service AS t8 ON t2.city_code = t8.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t8.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t9 ON t3.to_airport = t9.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t3.from_airport = t7.airport_code JOIN flight_fare AS t1 ON t3.flight_id = t1.flight_id JOIN city AS t6 ON t6.city_code = t7.city_code JOIN fare AS t5 ON t1.fare_id = t5.fare_id JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t9.city_code WHERE ( ( ( t2.city_name = "DALLAS" AND t4.city_name = "FORT WORTH" ) AND t3.flight_number = 852 ) AND t6.city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) AND t3.airline_code = "DL";

695. please tell me how many nonstop flights there are from BOSTON to ATLANTA

SELECT COUNT ( DISTINCT t5.flight_id ) FROM city AS t4 JOIN airport_service AS t1 ON t4.city_code = t1.city_code JOIN flight AS t5 ON t5.from_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t2 ON t5.to_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN city AS t3 ON t3.city_code = t2.city_code WHERE ( t4.city_name = "BOSTON" AND t3.city_name = "ATLANTA" ) AND t5.stops = 0;

727. los angeles to pittsburgh afternoon monday
P: los angeles to pittsburgh afternoon on monday

SELECT DISTINCT t3.flight_id FROM airport AS t1 JOIN airport_service AS t6 ON t1.airport_code = t6.airport_code JOIN city AS t5 ON t5.city_code = t6.city_code JOIN flight AS t3 ON t3.to_airport = t1.airport_code JOIN days AS t8 ON t3.flight_days = t8.days_code JOIN airport AS t2 ON t3.from_airport = t2.airport_code JOIN airport_service AS t7 ON t2.airport_code = t7.airport_code JOIN city AS t4 ON t4.city_code = t7.city_code WHERE t5.city_name = "pittsburgh" AND t4.city_name = "los angeles" AND t8.day_name = "monday" AND t3.departure_time BETWEEN 1200 AND 1800;

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE ( ( ( ( departure_time <= 1900 AND departure_time >= 1800 ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "NASHVILLE" ) ) ) AND from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "NEWARK" ) ) ) AND airline_code = "AA" );

757. please find a flight round trip from LOS ANGELES to TACOMA WASHINGTON with a stopover in SAN FRANCISCO not exceeding the price of 300 dollars for 6 10 1993

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE ( ( ( ( flight_days IN ( SELECT days_code FROM days WHERE day_name IN ( SELECT day_name FROM date_day WHERE day_number = 10 AND month_number = 6 AND year = 1993 ) ) AND flight_id IN ( SELECT flight_id FROM flight_fare WHERE fare_id IN ( SELECT fare_id FROM fare WHERE ( ( fare_basis_code IN ( SELECT fare_basis_code FROM fare_basis WHERE basis_days IN ( SELECT days_code FROM days WHERE day_name IN ( SELECT day_name FROM date_day WHERE day_number = 10 AND month_number = 6 AND year = 1991 ) ) ) AND round_trip_cost <= 300 ) AND round_trip_cost is NOT null ) ) ) ) AND flight_id IN ( SELECT flight_id FROM flight_stop WHERE stop_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "SAN FRANCISCO" ) ) ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE ( city_name = "TACOMA" AND state_code IN ( SELECT state_code FROM state WHERE state_name = "WASHINGTON" ) ) ) ) ) AND from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "LOS ANGELES" ) ) );

758. please find a flight from ONTARIO to WESTCHESTER COUNTY that makes a stop in CHICAGO on 5 17 one way with DINNER

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE ( ( ( ( ( flight_days IN ( SELECT days_code FROM days WHERE day_name IN ( SELECT day_name FROM date_day WHERE day_number = 17 AND month_number = 5 AND year = 1991 ) ) AND flight_id IN ( SELECT flight_id FROM flight_fare WHERE fare_id IN ( SELECT fare_id FROM fare WHERE ( fare_basis_code IN ( SELECT fare_basis_code FROM fare_basis WHERE basis_days IN ( SELECT days_code FROM days WHERE day_name IN ( SELECT day_name FROM date_day WHERE day_number = 17 AND month_number = 5 AND year = 1991 ) ) ) AND round_trip_required = "NO" ) ) ) ) AND meal_code IN ( SELECT meal_code FROM food_service WHERE meal_description = "DINNER" ) ) AND flight_id IN ( SELECT flight_id FROM flight_stop WHERE stop_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "CHICAGO" ) ) ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "WESTCHESTER COUNTY" ) ) ) AND from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "ONTARIO" ) ) );

759. is there one airline that flies from BURBANK to MILWAUKEE milwaukee to ST. LOUIS and from ST. LOUIS to BURBANK

SELECT DISTINCT airline_code FROM airline WHERE ( ( airline_code IN ( SELECT airline_code FROM flight WHERE ( from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "ST. LOUIS" ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "BURBANK" ) ) ) ) AND airline_code IN ( SELECT airline_code FROM flight WHERE ( from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "BURBANK" ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "MILWAUKEE" ) ) ) ) ) AND airline_code IN ( SELECT airline_code FROM flight WHERE ( from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "MILWAUKEE" ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "ST. LOUIS" ) ) ) ) );

760. i'd like to book two flights to WESTCHESTER COUNTY

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "WESTCHESTER COUNTY" ) );

761. find me a flight from CINCINNATI to any airport in the NEW YORK area

SELECT DISTINCT flight_id FROM flight WHERE ( from_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "CINCINNATI" ) ) AND to_airport IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport WHERE airport_code IN ( SELECT airport_code FROM airport_service WHERE city_code IN ( SELECT city_code FROM city WHERE city_name = "NEW YORK" ) ) ) );
